British Giant Ship Launched 37

Displacing 73,000 Tons

Named the Queen Mary

Glasgow: The largest passenger ship ever built by a British shipyard, the number (534), displacing 73,000 tons, was safely launched into the River Clyde today. The Queen of England attended the ceremony and named it the Queen Mary. Hundreds of thousands of people from all over the country came to watch the ceremony, and tens of thousands of others listened to the broadcast of the ceremony on the radio. The King and Queen, accompanied by the Crown Prince, departed from Balmoral Castle at 9:00 AM this morning and arrived here. At 2:50 PM, the shipyard of John Brown & Company ascended the imperial platform and received enthusiastic cheers from countless people. Kirkwood, a Labor Party member of the House of Commons, was most influential in the recommencement of work on this ship. Therefore, the directors of Cunard White Star Line first met the King and Queen to offer a welcome message, and the King replied as follows: (The storms of the ocean are treacherous and difficult to overcome, and their power is stronger than human beings, but in modern times, the struggle with the ocean has been matched. It has not been a hundred years since the late Cunard founded the wooden-hulled steamship to carry mail across the Atlantic. Today, there must be someone who remembers being surprised to hear about a steamship of 1,150 tons when they were young. Comparing the past with the present, we can see how human power has overcome nature. Today, we are honored to witness the launching of this giant ship that surpasses all others.) At this point, the King thanked all those who contributed to the construction of the ship, from dignitaries to laborers, and said that he had been concerned about the ship's three-year suspension of work, and he was now delighted to see it completed. He affirmed that (commerce on both sides of the Atlantic now has the hope of improving, and this ship will be able to make a great contribution to the revival of international trade. In the past, Cunard built ships to carry mail to English-speaking countries, and today, Cunard is building this ship to carry a large number of passengers to foreign countries, so that they can better understand each other. We use this ship to convey goodwill to all countries, and we wish this ship a life at sea that can unfold friendship among all countries.) At the time of the ceremony, there was a heavy rain, but hundreds of thousands of spectators stood and stared as the new ship was launched, which took only 60 seconds. The King, wearing a naval admiral's uniform, delivered his speech, and then the Queen performed the naming ceremony. At this time, the crowd was silent, and the Queen said into the microphone, (I name you Queen Mary.) At that time, the sound of cheering was deafening. The Queen broke a bottle of wine against the bow of the ship, and then pressed a button, and the ship moved. Six tugboats towed it into the river. The imperial viewing platform was shaped like a wheelhouse and had three thrones. 2,000 police officers maintained order along the route, and 3,000 ambulances were prepared. The workers who built the ship sat in a special viewing platform, and five shipwrights over the age of 50 were summoned by the King and others. After the new ship was launched, the King and others had refreshments. Those who came to watch the ceremony began to gather before dawn, although the strong winds made people uncomfortable, but the King

US Reconstruction Administration to Reorganize; Johnson's Resignation Approved 38

Facing criticism from all sides for handling labor disputes

Baruch favored as successor

The end of the separation of powers and the autocratic system

Hyde Park: General Hugh S. Johnson is to resign from his position as head of the National Recovery Administration today, thus immediately relinquishing his role as a dictator in the American business community. His resignation has been approved by President Roosevelt. Johnson will officially leave office on October 15. His letter of resignation states that he shares the same views as the President regarding the reorganization of the NRA and hopes that the President can also understand that his resignation is due to the fact that his position will become superfluous after the reorganization. However, he will continue to be loyal to the President and is willing to serve the President if circumstances permit. President Roosevelt's reply was very cordial, praising Johnson's spirit, courage, and various achievements, and expressing the hope that he can continue to serve the country after a period of rest. According to a statement from (Summer White House), Johnson's resignation is not due to disagreements with the President. However, political observers believe that the victory of NRA advisor Donald Richberg and his theory of cooperation between the government and the business community in governing industry is the real reason for Johnson's resignation. Yesterday, some people predicted that Johnson would be forced to resign and that the world-renowned financier Bernard Baruch would become the chairman of the committee, with other members including early "brain trust" members such as Moley and Richberg. Baruch has now relinquished all important positions and claims that he will devote himself to (writing). Therefore, although he has not yet made any statements, he will be able to take office immediately if appointed by the government. According to today's news, the reorganization plan of the NRA will be announced in Washington soon. (National Telegram, 25th)

Hyde Park: After General Johnson's resignation as head of the National Recovery Administration, it is now the opinion of people here tonight that the autocratic system of the NRA will come to an end. The reorganization plan of the NRA will divide the powers concentrated in Johnson into three parts. First, there will be a council to determine the policies of the NRA, composed of representatives from the government, the industrial sector, and labor organizations. Second, there will be an executive committee to implement the policies set by the council. Third, there will be a legal department to handle litigation matters related to violations of regulations. Now that Johnson has resigned, the policy changes and reorganization of the NRA have not been announced. However, according to tonight's news, President Roosevelt will retain the ban on child labor and wage standards, while granting the industrial sector some autonomy. (National Telegram, 25th)

(New York): President Roosevelt will arrive in Washington tomorrow to discuss everything with Johnson. Before leaving office, Johnson will also make a final report to President Roosevelt. In recent months, Johnson's measures have been heavily criticized, and he has had disagreements with Labor Secretary Frances Perkins. Therefore, his resignation was expected. It is widely believed that Johnson's handling of the textile labor dispute was criticized as inappropriate in some respects, which is also one of the reasons for Johnson's resignation. This morning, New York newspapers reported that the film industry is considering hiring Johnson for a certain position with an annual salary of $100,000. There are currently three hopefuls to succeed Johnson as head of the NRA: Bernard Baruch, a well-known New York financier; Professor Moley, a former member of President Roosevelt's brain trust; and Swope, the deputy director of the NRA. (Reuters Telegram, 25th)

Evidence Conclusive that Lindbergh Kidnapping Case Suspect Received Ransom Money 40

(New York): Although Hauptmann still claims to be innocent in the kidnapping and murder of the Lindbergh baby today, the prosecutor has declared that there is evidence that Hauptmann received $50,000 in ransom money from Lindbergh. Lawyer Foley declared that detectives who searched Hauptmann's bedroom discovered that he had been in contact with Dr. Condon, who served as an intermediary in the ransom negotiations. In addition to finding $13,750 in gold certificates from the ransom money in Hauptmann's bedroom, Dr. Condon's address and phone number were also found on the wall. Hauptmann has admitted that the address and phone numbers on the wall were written by him as a memento. There are many nails found in Hauptmann's house, some of which are of the same type as those used to build the wooden ladder used to access the Lindbergh baby's bedroom during the kidnapping. Coal Miner Strike Brewing in South Wales, UK 41

(London): There are over 130,000 coal miners in the South Wales coal region, and a strike is looming. Labor and management have been negotiating new wages in Cardiff for a long time, but have not yet reached a resolution. If an agreement cannot be reached within three days, a work stoppage on October 1st seems inevitable. The Coal Owners' Association issued an article stating that the previous meeting had completely reached a deadlock, and the coal owners are not prepared to increase the minimum wage. The current minimum wage is only 12.25% higher than in 1914, while the National Industrial Board advocates an increase of 20% to 28%. However, the coal owners insist that they are already paying 20% and cannot increase it further. They are willing to submit the dispute to an impartial and independent committee organized by the Ministry of Labor. The Miners' Federation is scheduled to hold a general meeting on the 28th of this month, and its final decision will be announced the following day. Secretary for Mines Ernest Brown has now invited representatives from labor and management to London by the 27th of this month to discuss solutions in order to eliminate obstacles and reach a resolution. (Reuters Telegram, 26th)

(London): The Gresford coal mine in North Wales exploded last Saturday, killing 260 people. It was the third largest mine disaster of this century. Because the fire in the mine was difficult to extinguish, the mine entrance was closed. Unexpectedly, the fire and gas under the mine spewed out from the cracks in the closure today. With a roar, it knocked an employee twenty yards away from where he was standing, seriously injuring him, and there is no hope of survival. The work of sealing the mine entrance must be implemented once again. As a result of this disaster, 2,500 workers will be directly and indirectly unemployed for one to three months. Most tragically, over 700 children are now orphans. The City of London has begun to raise funds to provide relief, and donations are pouring in from all over the country, with some donations as high as several five pounds. (Reuters Telegram, 25th)

| Reuters Special Commercial Telegram, September 26 |

Gold and Silver: London Gold Price - Today's gold price is 141 shillings and 3 pence, up half a penny from yesterday.

London Silver: London silver market is up 25 today. Spot price is 22 pence 3125, futures is 22 pence 375. Chinese sellers are fewer, while Indian and speculators are still buying more, so the market price rose. Market conditions were uncertain at the close.

Bombay Silver: The Bombay silver market was calm this morning. Spot and October futures are both 60 rupees 10 annas, November futures 60 rupees 12 annas, all up 1 anna.

Exchange Rates: US-UK - There was continued demand for US dollars in the London foreign exchange market this morning. The opening US-UK exchange rate was 4 dollars 96 and 125/1000 cents, 75 less than yesterday's US-UK exchange rate close. It rose 0625 at 11 o'clock, but soon fell again to 4 dollars 96 and 0625/1000 cents. At 2 PM, it rose 0625 again, to 4 dollars 96 and 125/1000 cents. There was no action to maintain the exchange rate in the market today.

US-France - The opening rate was 74 francs 65, lower than yesterday's close by 6 pounds. At 1 PM, it fell another 6 pounds. At 2 PM, the exchange rate rose to 74 francs 65, the same as the opening price. There was no action to maintain the exchange rate in the market today.

US-UK - The pound continued to fall in the New York foreign exchange market this morning. The opening US-UK exchange rate was lower by 625/10000 and was 4 dollars 96 and 25/100 cents. Since then, the market has been very quiet and there is no change at the time of dispatch.

Cotton and Wheat: New York Cotton - At the opening of the cotton market, sales by spot merchants were offset by purchases from Liverpool and peers. Although the market was quiet, prices rose by 3 points. Hedging was scarce, and the price continued to rise by 1 point. At 10:40, spot merchants started selling again, and the price fell by 2 to 5 points.

Bombay Cotton - The Bombay cotton market rose due to the lack of short covering and purchases by various parties and European exporters. The closing price for April-May Balaji cotton was 213 rupees, up 3 and a half rupees.

Liverpool Cotton - The Liverpool cotton market also rose today. At 1 PM, the October futures price was 6.78, up 6 points.

New York Wheat - Although the Liverpool price rose, the opening price of the Chicago wheat market was down 125/1000. Unfavorable weather in Canada led people to believe the market was oversold, so although the May futures continued to fall 125/1000, the near-term futures rose 125/1000.

Liverpool Wheat - Prices soared today. At 1 PM, the October futures price was 5 shillings 1 and 875/1000 pence, higher than yesterday's close by 1 and 125/1000 pence.

Rubber: London - The rubber market was quiet this morning. At noon, the transaction price for October-December futures was 7 pence 4375/10000, the same as yesterday's closing price.

New York - The rubber market opened under pressure from selling rumors, falling 11 to 13 points. The market felt a little chaotic, and prices rose by 3 points, then fell by 5 points shortly after.

Securities: New York - The favorable factors for the market before the opening of securities were: (1) After the resignation of Hugh S. Johnson, the director of the National Recovery Administration, it is expected that President Roosevelt will announce the reorganization of the Recovery Administration within a few days, which is beneficial to both commerce and the market. (2) The new regulations on securities trading margin are not expected to be very stringent, which greatly excites the bulls. Yesterday's price rebound and the increase in trading after the price increase are signs of a good market. The unfavorable factors for the market are: (1) Textile mills are resuming operations slowly due to a lack of orders. (2) Unstable foreign exchange. The market was more active and stable at the opening of securities this morning than before. Although there were occasional profit-takings, sentiment was better than yesterday. The Steps of Japanese and Puppet Activities in Our Western Mongolia 86

Dispatching Personnel to Threaten Princes and Lamas

Surveying the Mountains and Terrain of Each Banner

Special dispatch from Suiyuan: Since the Japanese and puppet troops occupied Dolon in May last year, they have never stopped thinking about advancing into various parts of Western Mongolia, including the Twelve Banners of (Chahar), the Seven Banners of the Xilingol League (Suiyuan), the Six Banners of the Ulanqab League, the Seven Banners of the Yekejuu League, the Tumet Independent Banner (Ningxia), and the Alxa Independent Banner, all within their plan. The methods are roughly divided into three stages: The first stage (military aggression) in the summer of last year, Japanese and puppet troops and a small number of Mongolians marched west from Chengde and Dolon to the various banners of Chahar and Xilingol bordering Rehe under the pretext of suppressing bandits, hoping to gain an inch and then a foot. Unexpectedly, as soon as the Japanese and puppet troops entered Western Mongolia, the local Mongolians, princes, and governors were shocked, giving Western Mongolia an impression of aversion to evil. The Japanese and puppets then changed their strategy and used the second stage (method of inducement) last year. However, the Mongolians of the Twelve Banners of Chahar were the first to be enlightened and were mostly unmoved. Although the banners of the Xilingol League were less knowledgeable, they were also deeply afraid of the Japanese and dared not approach them. Moreover, the leaders of the western part of the Xilingol League, such as Prince De, were advocating Mongolian autonomy, which was even more incompatible with the Japanese side's propaganda of inducement. Because the second phase method failed, the Japanese and puppets used the third stage (resolute measures) and harassed in various ways. The Sokh Prince's Mansion in the Left Wing of the East Ujimqin Banner in the northeast of the Xilingol League (Sokh is the head of the Xilingol League) is adjacent to Rehe. After a long period of harassment by the Japanese and puppets last winter, its palace was forcibly set up with a radio station, and a Japanese lived permanently in the palace, appearing as if he were the master. This summer, the Japanese came to the Lama Temple of Beizi Chao in the east of Xilingol and forcibly set up a radio station. Eight Japanese, two Mongolian clerks, and two old banner people from Beiping were stationed in the temple for a long time, and established a puppet country's special agent commissioner's office in the temple, with the same organization as Dolon, with great power, responsible for major missions such as military, diplomatic, and investigation, and its subordinates have been more active in various parts of Western Mongolia since the summer of this year. On the one hand, they went to various princes and Lama temples to publicize the foreign policy of the puppet state, and on the other hand, they went to various banners in Western Mongolia to investigate mountains and terrain in batches. At the beginning of this month, the special agent commissioner of Beizi Temple suddenly dispatched more than ten cars, several civil and military officials, and more than ten Mongolian soldiers to Prince De's mansion in Bangjiang, requesting Prince De to negotiate. At that time, Prince De was returning to the mansion from Bailingmiao, and only left the mansion to return to the temple last week. According to a traveler from Bangjiang, the Japanese came this time to set up a radio station in the east of the Prince's mansion and to discuss the establishment of the so-called North China Hospital in the Prince's mansion. As for how Prince De dealt with it, the outside world does not yet know. The puppet country's ambition to encroach on Western Mongolia has been repeatedly exposed.

Recently, the number of Japanese who have come to Zhangjiakou under the pretext of investigation and travel has been increasing. They are all claimed to be conducting investigations. It is heard that Military Officer Matsui recently came to Zhangjiakou from Rehe in his personal capacity and rented a house belonging to a certain surname in front of the railway, with the words "Matsui Residence" pasted on the gate. This action must have a special purpose. There is also Mr. Shengdao, a Japanese who has lived in Zhangjiakou for many years, 50 years old, who is the current chief of the Special Agent Office of Beizi Temple in Western Mongolia. Recently, he has been frequently traveling between Changchun and Beizi Temple, directing all work. His residence in Zhangjiakou is on Shahe Road in Tou'ergou. He married a Chinese woman as his wife, whose family is originally from Wanquan County, thirty li north of Zhangjiakou.

Preparations for the Office of the Mongolian Political Guidance Commissioner 87

Men Bingyue and Chun Heming Ordered to Go to Bailingmiao for Consultation

Scope of Organization Will Be Smaller Than Originally Planned

Dispatch from Beiping: The Mongolian Local Autonomy Political Affairs Committee will have been established for half a year. In the past five months, autonomous political affairs have been unsuccessful due to (1) the indefinite assumption of office by the Guidance Commissioner and (2) the failure to receive political funding on time. Since General He Yingqin, Chairman of the Military Branch of the Committee, was appointed as the concurrent Guidance Commissioner, the delay in assuming office has its own difficulties that must be considered. Since General He has been stationed in Beiping, his responsibilities have been very heavy. He has been busy day and night and has had no free time. Moreover, the complexity of Mongolian affairs cannot be handled by remote guidance. Therefore, he has repeatedly declined and telegraphed the Central Government to appoint another capable person. On the other hand, the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee was bewildered by the indefinite assumption of office by the Guidance Commissioner. Envoys traveled incessantly on the Ping-Sui Road, expressing their sincerity in supporting General He in addition to urging him to assume office as soon as possible. The Central Government also repeatedly telegraphed General He to assume office as soon as possible, so as to relieve the Central Government's concern for the north. After repeated telegraphic communications, General He has now decided to send Men Bingyue, a senior counselor of the Military Branch of the Committee, and others to Bailingmiao to meet with Yun Duanwangchuk, Chairman of the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee, and Prince De, a member of the Committee, De Wangde. Men is scheduled to take the Pingbao through train to Suiyuan at 7:00 AM tomorrow (26th). Several members of the General Staff of the Military Branch of the Committee will also accompany him. According to sources, Men and others will stay in Suiyuan for a considerable period of time when they return from Bailingmiao, so that they can report the results of the consultations in the temple to General He and await further instructions.

It is also learned that Men and others are going to Suiyuan under the order of General He to prepare for the establishment of the Office of the Guidance Commissioner. The reason for going to Bailingmiao first is that on the one hand, they will represent General He in extending greetings to all members of the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee and, as convenient, inform them that General He has decided to telegraph the Central Government to request monthly payments of funds to the Mongolian Political Affairs Committee to avoid stagnation in political affairs. Regarding the scope of the organization of the Office of the Guidance Commissioner, due to financial reasons, the original organization will be reduced accordingly. The content is divided into offices, with sections established below. Some of the candidates for the positions of director and section chief have already been internally decided, and General He will issue a clear order when he actually assumes office in the future. Regarding the address of the Office of the Commissioner, it has been generally decided to locate it in Suiyuan. After the organization of the office is ready, General He will take an oath of office in Beiping on a scheduled date, lead the political office remotely, and send Men Bingyue to station in Suiyuan to take responsibility for transmission. As for General He's personal visit to Suiyuan, as of the time of dispatch, the relevant parties have stated that there are no such preparations. According to general speculation, General He's trip to Suiyuan may only be a matter of time. It is also unknown, because since the Office of the Guidance Commissioner is planned to be established in Suiyuan, it would be appropriate for General He to personally inspect it. (25th)

衍聖公孔德成拒絶日人誘惑 88

Japanese Toyota Visits Qufu, Refused Meeting by Kong

Kong Clan to Release Statement

Shandong Province Conference on Repairing the Confucius Temple is Underway

Jinan Correspondence: Japanese recently suddenly advocate venerating Confucius, in addition to greatly repairing the Confucius Temple, also planning to hold a Confucius sacrificial ceremony next spring. According to a dispatch from the Japanese United News Agency on the 21st of this month, Japan has decided to hold a Confucius sacrificial ceremony next spring, inviting over a hundred prominent scholars from China, Korea, and Taiwan to hold a grand Eastern academic lecture, placing our country alongside Korea and Taiwan, which were forcibly occupied by the Japanese. This is extremely insulting to us. The news agency also said that the 77th generation descendant of Confucius, the Duke Yansheng, his uncle Kong Lingcan, descendants of the Meng and Yan families, and leading Confucian scholars of the time will be invited to Japan to participate, etc. The Japanese's actions are harboring ulterior motives. If Confucius knew, he would never accept the sacrificial rites of the tyrannical Japanese. Even Kong Decheng, who has received considerable education, and Kong Lingcan, currently the head of the First Section of the Education Bureau, would certainly not be obsequious and go to Japan to participate in the Confucius sacrificial ceremony at a time when our national humiliation is still unavenged. According to Kong Lingcan, regarding this matter, he has recently learned of something else that can corroborate this. A Japanese man named Toyota once went to Qufu to request an audience with Kong Decheng, but was refused. Kong Decheng also resolved not to receive any Japanese who come to Qufu in the future, to avoid complications. Based on this, it is evident that the Japanese are not merely engaging in propaganda but actually want to implement their deceptive policy. Their intention is not only to insult but must have other purposes. In the future, the Kong clan will have to issue a statement to the world, publicly denying this. Kong Decheng, being educated and cultured, would definitely not allow himself to be fooled by the Japanese and bring shame upon the sage, etc.

Further news: Civil Affairs Director Li Shuchun and Education Director He Siyuan proposed repairing the Kuiwen Pavilion of the Confucius Temple to create an ancient artifact exhibition hall, which was approved by the provincial government. A letter was sent to the Confucius Temple Repair Preparatory Committee to inform them. Today (the 25th), the preparatory committee held a meeting in the West Flower Hall of the provincial government, chaired by Han Fuju. (A) Matters reported: (1) Since the 13th standing committee meeting, 2,000 yuan in foreign currency was received from Chen Jitang, bringing the total to 4,022.05 yuan. It was resolved to deposit it in the Minsheng Bank. (2) A telegram from Qingdao Mayor Shen Honglie on the 20th stated that he was honored to be appointed as honorary vice president for the repair of the Confucius Temple and would do his best to contribute to the grand undertaking. It was resolved to file it. (3) A letter from the provincial government, based on a submission from the provincial secretariat, stated that the funds donated for the repair of the Yan Temple in Qufu were insufficient to cover expenses, and requested instructions on which item to allocate funds from. After deliberation, it was resolved to first use the existing donations for repairs. The Construction Department was instructed to comply and informed accordingly. It was resolved to file it. (B) Matters for discussion: (1) A letter from the Construction Department forwarding a report from technician Yang Judou stating that he was ordered to inspect the trees growing on the roof of the Confucius Temple. After detailed inspection, there were three locations with trees growing, listed below: (1) Dacheng Hall: A cluster of about five or six trees, all about two meters tall and three or four centimeters in diameter, growing under the front eaves between the roof tiles. (2) Dacheng Gate: A cluster of about four or five trees, about 1.7 or 1.8 meters tall and three or four centimeters in diameter, growing on the roof ridge of the rear eaves. (3) Kuiwen Pavilion: A elm tree, about 3.5 meters tall and six or seven centimeters in diameter, and over ten smaller trees, all about one meter tall and two or three centimeters in diameter, growing under the rear eaves between the roof tiles. There were at least seven or eight other places with trees or grass growing on the roof, but not as large as the three locations above. In view of the previous instructions, the inspection situation was submitted for review. It was resolved to have the Confucius Temple Repair Committee assess and handle the situation. It was resolved to estimate the cost of repairs. (2) A telegram from Dai Chuanxian on the 3rd stated that the repair of the Confucius Temple was a great undertaking to revive the national spirit, and he felt unworthy to be the chairman due to his limited abilities, but would do his best to assist. He asked how to proceed and requested a public decision. It was resolved to file it. (3) A letter from the provincial government stated that at the political affairs meeting of the department, committee members Li and He proposed allocating the remaining funds from the Yan Temple repair to repair the Kuiwen Pavilion of the Confucius Temple and establish an ancient artifact exhibition hall. After discussion, it was resolved to send a letter to the Confucius Temple Repair Preparatory Committee to dispatch personnel for surveying and estimation, and requested instructions on how to proceed. It was resolved that the funds for the Yan Temple project were from over 30,000 yuan allocated from the donations received for the Confucius Temple repair, with the Construction Department allocating funds for construction and no remaining funds. The meeting was then adjourned.

Anhui Province to Implement Lifting of Rice and Grain Export Ban 89

Detailed Investigation Shows Food Supply Still Sufficient

Plan to Collect Rice Tax to Allow Export from the Province

Wuhu Correspondence: Due to the drought in Anhui Province, the provincial government has followed the example of the major flood of the 20th year of the Republic and implemented a ban on rice exports to maintain the food supply for the people. It has also organized a Food Regulation Committee and dispatched investigation team director Li Zhenya to various places to investigate the amount of rice in storage. Li's investigation showed that although many counties had suffered poor harvests, the number of polder fields was quite large, and the overall food supply seemed to be still sufficient. Moreover, other provinces were already experiencing food shortages and had lifted the ban on trade, which would greatly benefit the rural economy of this province. He truthfully reported this to the provincial government and proposed collecting an export tax on rice and allowing rice to be exported from the province. The revenue from this tax would be used for drought relief. Rice merchants also hoped that the export of rice would be permitted, as it would greatly revitalize commerce and finance. Collecting the tax would clearly indicate restrictions and would not affect the food supply. It is expected that around five million shi (a unit of dry volume) could be exported by both steamer and sailboat. It is said that the provincial government has reviewed the proposal and has decided to implement it. It plans to collect a tax of 4 jiao (a unit of currency) per shi for steamer exports, collected in Wuhu, and 1 yuan per shi for sailboat exports, with an office set up in Heshang Port to handle it. However, the undecided matter is that at a time when harsh taxes and miscellaneous levies are being abolished, likin and surcharges are strictly prohibited. The name and method are still under consideration. The planned implementation date is October 1st. Initially, due to the severity of the drought, it was also planned to pre-borrow 1 million yuan from rice merchants in this area to fund disaster relief, with the rice tax used as collateral. Rice merchants felt uneasy because the rice market has been exhausted for several years and they could not raise such a large sum in a short period of time. After repeated consultations, it was decided to borrow 60,000 yuan to provide urgent relief. However, what worries rice merchants is whether rice and grain will be allowed to pass through Jiangsu Province in the future, even if Anhui Province permits the export. (24th)

Over 300,000 Mu of Disaster-Stricken Fields in the County 92

After Jiangsu Province announced the disaster assessment measures, it immediately ordered the district chiefs to instruct the Tu district secretaries and township chiefs to prepare disaster registers listing the number of completely barren and partially barren mu within the county and submit them to the county. Chinese Silk Listed Intermittently in the US 93

In recent years, Chinese silk has suffered a sharp decline in the market due to obstacles to overseas sales. Although the government has tried to provide relief, it has been difficult to reverse the trend due to the global economic situation. In May of this year, the New York Mercantile Exchange in the United States allowed Chinese silk to be listed and to be used as a substitute for Japanese silk in deliveries. To regain its original market share in the United States, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and various silk manufacturers in China ordered the Shanghai Standard Inspection Bureau to conduct rigorous inspections of export silk. However, after Chinese silk was listed in the US, Japanese merchants dumped silk at discounted prices. Chinese merchants, with limited economic strength and relying mostly on outdated manufacturing methods, had to suspend trading after just over ten days. Through the efforts of the Chinese Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Chinese silk merchants, trading has now resumed intermittently.

Land Price Declaration Case Takes a Sudden Turn 94

Since the Wuxi Land Price Declaration Office sent personnel to carry out declarations from house to house in the city and suburbs, the process initially proceeded smoothly. However, as soon as people heard that land price tax and land price appreciation tax would be levied after the land declaration, they became suspicious and fearful, and dared not declare. Moreover, land in Wuxi has not been surveyed since the land survey during the reign of Emperor Tongzhi of the Qing Dynasty, over seventy years ago. There are many discrepancies in household numbers, and even the declaration of mu is difficult. Therefore, everyone adopted a wait-and-see attitude. Recently, Chairman Chen of the Jiangsu Provincial Government stated that the land price declaration was in accordance with President Chiang Kai-shek's intention to benefit the people, and was originally intended to develop people's livelihood and promote social prosperity. Local people should understand this and cooperate. He specially summoned County Magistrate Yan Shenyu to the province to explain the matter. Qian Jihou, director of the County Property Office, also sent a letter to the county government, stating that what the public organizations and local people feared and suspected was not the land price declaration itself, but the levying of land price tax and land price appreciation tax after the declaration was completed. The current market is depressed, and the economy has plummeted. He requested that the difficulties of the people be considered and that a request be forwarded to the provincial government to postpone the land price tax and land price appreciation tax until the market recovers and autonomy is achieved. County Magistrate Yan returned to Wuxi yesterday morning (26th). It is reported that the provincial government has indicated that it will consider postponing the land price tax. Representatives of various public organizations, including Li Tiping, Qian Sunqing, and Yang Hanxi, are scheduled to convene local people, district chiefs, and township chiefs at the Chamber of Commerce this afternoon (27th) to discuss the matter. The land price declaration, which had been stalled due to disagreements, has now taken a sudden turn.

Sun and Wang Discuss Constitution 101

Not Drafting a Separate Proposal

Regarding the recent visit of Legislative Yuan President Sun Ke to Shanghai to discuss constitutional issues with Dr. Wang Chonghui, the reporter investigated the situation yesterday and found that Sun has always advocated an open approach to the constitution-making process. He repeatedly published the initial draft and revised draft to solicit opinions from across the country and appointed three committee members, Chuan Bingchang, Tao Lüqian, and Lin Bin, to conduct a dedicated review. As Dr. Wang Chonghui, known for his expertise in law and former legal advisor to the Legislative Yuan, had returned from Europe, Sun assigned Chuan Bingchang, Tao Lüqian, and Lin Bin to come to Shanghai and discuss everything with Wang. Wang met with Chuan, Tao, and Lin over the past two days for detailed discussions, which have yielded significant results. It is said that the presidential system will still be adopted, but the National Assembly Committee will be removed. Chuan and the others plan to return to Beijing with Sun on Thursday evening to further refine the clauses in order to present them at the Legislative Yuan's plenary session this Friday. The report in the newspaper the day before yesterday that Chuan had integrated Sun and Wang's opinions to draft a separate proposal was hearsay and not factual.

Yuping Railway Loan Contract to be Finalized and Signed Today 103

Agreement Reached with Banking Syndicate for Advance Withdrawal

Yunan Section Already Put Out to Tender, Scheduled for Completion by End of Next Year

Zeng Yangfu Continued Discussions Yesterday Regarding Materials

New Sound News Agency reports: The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Joint Company held its fourth board meeting at the Bank of China in Shanghai the day before yesterday and negotiated the contract with the Yuping Railway loan syndicate. The contract has now been finalized and is scheduled to be signed today. The loan has been agreed to by the banking syndicate, and advance withdrawals have been approved. The details are as follows:

Continued Discussions Yesterday: The Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Joint Company continued to exchange views with representatives of the banking syndicate, including Bank of China General Manager Zhang Gongquan, yesterday morning, after negotiating the Yuping Railway mortgage loan contract the day before. Those present included Chairman Zeng Yangfu, directors Wu Jiantao, Gong Xuesui, Xiao Chunjin, Chen Yaozu, and Zheng Hua, as well as Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau Deputy Director Hou Jiayuan and Board Secretary Chen Xiaocen. The contract negotiated the day before was reviewed and finalized, and the meeting adjourned at 11:30 AM.

Bank Banquet: Banks in Shanghai, including the Bank of China, Shanghai Bank, Jincheng Bank, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Xinhua Bank, and Jiangxi Yumin Bank, as well as the General Administration of Postal Savings and Remittances, jointly hosted a banquet at the Jincheng Bank on Jiangxi Road at 12:00 PM yesterday. Attendees included Zeng Yangfu, Wu Jiantao, Gong Xuesui, Xiao Chunjin, Chen Yaozu, Zheng Hua, Hou Jiayuan, Chen Xiaocen, Zhang Gongquan, Wu Yunchu, Zou Bingwen, Wang Zhixin, and Xu Baiyuan. The banquet ended happily at 2:00 PM.

Bank Responsibilities: A reporter from New Sound News Agency interviewed Zeng Yangfu, Director of the Zhejiang Construction Department, at the New Asia Hotel at 5:00 PM yesterday and was informed that to build the Yuping Railway, the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Joint Company will mortgage 12 million yuan each of the First Phase Railway Construction Bonds and Yuping Railway Bonds to banks such as the Bank of China for a loan of 8 million yuan. The Bank of China will be responsible for 3.75 million yuan, Jincheng Bank for 1.5 million yuan, Shanghai Bank for 1 million yuan, Zhejiang Industrial Bank for 500,000 yuan, Xinhua Bank for 500,000 yuan, Jiangxi Yumin Bank for 500,000 yuan, and the General Administration of Postal Savings and Remittances for 250,000 yuan. The annual interest rate is 1%, and the loan will be repaid in five years.

Materials Loan: In addition to mortgaging the above bonds to banks for 8 million yuan, the same bonds will be mortgaged to the German Otto Wolff factory for a materials loan of 8 million yuan, with the banking syndicate providing credit guarantees and holding the bonds in custody. The material prices have now been agreed upon, and the required materials will be shipped to China from Germany as needed. The Yunan section is now under construction, and some of the required materials have already begun shipping from Germany.

Segmented Construction: The construction of the Yuping Railway will be divided into the Yushan to Nanchang section and the Nanchang to Pingxiang section. It has now been decided to build the Yushan to Nanchang section first, which is approximately 340 kilometers long and has already been put out to tender and construction has begun. It is scheduled for completion and opening to traffic by the end of next year. As for the Nanchang to Pingxiang section, which is approximately 300 kilometers long, it has been decided to start construction after the Yushan to Nanchang section is completed. In the future, it will be connected to the Hangzhou-Jiangshan Railway and be collectively known as the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Bureau.

Signing Today: The banks providing the loan will form the Yuping Railway Loan Syndicate and designate the Bank of China as the syndicate representative. The contract has now been negotiated and finalized and is scheduled to be signed tomorrow (today). The signatories will be Zeng Yangfu, Chairman of the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Joint Company, and Zhang Gongquan and Zhou Zuomin, representatives of the banking syndicate, for a total of more than ten copies, with each participating bank holding a copy.

Advance Withdrawal: After the construction of the Yunan section began, construction funds were needed. The banking syndicate has agreed to allow advance withdrawals of some of the agreed amount. Finally, the reporter inquired about the date of return to Hangzhou and was informed that he would return to Hangzhou after the contract is signed tomorrow (today). It is reported that the amount of the Yuping Railway mortgage loan that has been withdrawn to date is over 4 million yuan.

Materials Negotiations: Zeng Yangfu, Director of the Zhejiang Construction Department, met with three German representatives of the German Otto Wolff factory, which is providing the materials loan, in the reception room on the fourth floor of the New Asia Hotel at 3:00 PM yesterday. The meeting ended around 4:00 PM. It is said that the meeting was to report on the shipment of materials to China. The materials loan contract was signed separately between the banking syndicate and the German Otto Wolff factory, stipulating that the banking syndicate will provide credit guarantees and hold the bonds in custody. The materials price list is attached to the contract signed between the Zhejiang-Jiangxi Railway Company and the banking syndicate.

Chen Youbo, Manager of Shun'an Company, Plotted to Blow Up Shun'an Wheel Unsuccessfully 106

The Ship Was Detained by the Customs of Sanduao

Manager Chen Youbo Was the Mastermind

Plotting to Blow Up the Ship to Obtain Compensation

Ship Owner Reported to the Customs

Chen Has Been Arrested and Sent to the Police Station

The Shun'an wheel of Shun'an Company in Dunhouli, Zhonghua Road, Shanghai, was fully loaded with more than 1,500 tons of goods on the 14th and sailed to Xinghua, Quanzhou, for unloading. When the ship sailed, Chen Youbo, the manager of the Shanghai branch, instructed the ship owner to increase the insurance amount and secretly detonated explosives, intending to sink the ship and obtain compensation. The reporter personally investigated this shocking news from all sides, and the details are as follows:

Dedicated to Xinghua and Quanzhou Routes: The Shun'an Shipping Company was organized by Zheng Zhongwu (a Fujian native, currently a special member of the Central People's Movement Guidance Committee), Chen Youbo (a native of Xinghua, Fujian), and others. Zheng Zhongwu serves as the chairman, and Chen Youbo serves as the manager of the Shanghai headquarters. It has been open for five or six years. They purchased a Shun'an wheel (formerly the Fusheng), with a net tonnage of 1,177 tons. They have a marine safety insurance of 60,000 yuan with the China United Insurance Company and a deposit of 15,000 yuan with the Hua'an Insurance Company. It operates between Shanghai, Xinghua, and Quanzhou in Fujian, specializing in various groceries. Branch offices are set up in Xinghua and Quanzhou to manage passenger and cargo transportation between Shanghai and Xinghua. The business is quite prosperous.

Manager Suddenly Conceived a Malicious Plan: All the company's power is managed by Chen Youbo. In terms of shipping, it is not likely to lose money. However, Chen Youbo also engages in other speculative businesses on weekdays, and the losses are increasing. Recently, he felt that there was no way to make up for it, so he suddenly had evil thoughts and secretly decided on a malicious plan. Taking advantage of this time when the Shun'an wheel was transporting goods from Shanghai to Xingquan, Chen Youbo specially purchased explosive white medicine cans, intending to order the Shun'an ship owner Ouyang Tai to take out insurance for 1,000 tons of cargo when the ship set sail. When the ship reached outside the Wusongkou, he would detonate the ship, intending to get compensation of about 100,000 yuan.

Agreement to Split the Money Four to Six: When planning this ship bombing, Chen Youbo secretly invited the ship owner Ouyang Tai to discuss it in person. He handed over four cans of explosives and ordered him to detonate the ship as soon as it left Wusong. When the compensation was received in the future, he was willing to reward him with 40%. At that time, Ouyang Tai was forced by the manager's power and did not dare to refuse, so he had to verbally accept the order. He took four cans of explosives and went on board. On the 14th, he set sail from Shanghai to Xingquan.

Ship Owner Pretended to Be Sick on the Way: The ship owner was fundamentally opposed to this matter, but he could not cope with it. Therefore, after the Shun'an wheel sailed out of Wusong, he pretended to be sick on the ship and entrusted the driving to the first and second mates, Sheng Fuchen and Wang Daoji, to manage. Ouyang Tai never told the crew about this matter after arriving on the ship. When the ship arrived at the Wenzhou sea area, the first and second mates reported the voyage to Ouyang Tai, but the ship owner still did not announce the matter.

Surrendered to Sanduao Customs: On the 18th of this month, when the Shun'an wheel was sailing to Sanduao, the ship owner thought that the ship was about to arrive in Quanzhou. If this matter was not announced, the reported export goods would not match, and the customers would definitely pursue it. If the ship was bombed according to Chen Youbo's malicious plan, the relationship would be too great. After repeated consideration, he weighed the pros and cons and told the first and second mates, Sheng and Wang, the detailed reasons for the matter and discussed how to deal with it. After the three discussed, they had to surrender to the Sanduao Customs. They sailed the Shun'an wheel to Sanduao and sent the first mate Sheng Fuchen to report to the Customs.

People and Ships Were Detained Together: After receiving the report, the Sanduao Customs believed that the circumstances were very serious. They immediately detained the Shun'an wheel and the ship owner Ouyang Tai. All the explosives used by Chen Youbo to bomb the entire ship were seized. They immediately sent a secret telegram to Shanghai to investigate the case thoroughly. It was found that the Shun'an wheel was mostly loaded with flour, followed by soybeans, cigarettes, and miscellaneous goods. They are now also blocked in Sanduao. In recent days, many customers and cargo owners have been inquiring about the matter with the company.

Chen Youbo Has Been Arrested: After the Shun'an wheel was detained, Chen Youbo, the Shanghai manager, got the news and took the opportunity to abscond. The company's affairs were suspended. At the same time, Zheng Zhongwu, the chairman of the company, believed that the manager's improper behavior had discredited the company. He specially sent someone to Chen Youbo's residence at No. 57, Tongshouli, Datong Road, Avenue Edward VII, to look for him, but he was nowhere to be found. Therefore, he reported to the Public Security Bureau and other police agencies to track him down. He was finally arrested by Zheng Zhongwu on the way in Lujiazui at 2 pm the day before yesterday and sent to the police station. There were only three or four staff and students in the company. The rest of the important staff had all absconded. Chen Youbo has been detained by the French Concession police and will be sent to court for interrogation.

Insurance Statement of Withdrawal: The Shun'an wheel of Shun'an Shipping Company is insured for 60,000 yuan by the China Ship Insurance Association at No. 38, Avenue Edward VII. The company also pledged 15,000 yuan to the Hua'an Insurance Company on Jing'an Temple Road. According to Tang Danhua, the manager of the China Insurance Association, although it has not been confirmed whether it was a fraud to obtain compensation, there is indeed a situation of mutual contention among the crew members. It is found that sailing a ship is not comparable to land. A slight oversight can lead to the danger of hitting a reef or sinking. Now that this kind of secret has been discovered among the crew members, the Association has declared that it will withdraw from the insurance to avoid future disputes. All documents are declared invalid.

Navigation Bureau Thoroughly Investigated and Awaited Punishment: The Shanghai Maritime Affairs Bureau of the Ministry of Communications was suspicious after receiving a non-official report the day before yesterday. It was believed that the ship owner Ouyang Tai was honest and capable and would never commit the illegal act of colluding to blow up the ship. Later, after the wife of the first mate Sheng Fuchen brought Sheng's personal letter to report to the Maritime Affairs Bureau, they sent someone to the Jianghai Customs to investigate yesterday. The ship was indeed detained by the Sanduao Customs. Therefore, the Maritime Affairs Bureau is now investigating the truth in detail to impose punishment.

Ministry of Railways Replies to the Chamber of Commerce Explaining That State Coal Is Responsible for Transportation 115

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce previously received a letter from the Coal Industry Association stating that both roads were handling responsible transportation, increasing the price of coal per catty, and merchants and people could not bear the burden. They immediately submitted it to the Ministry of Railways, requesting that it be transferred to maintain the old price and charge. The original text was published in various newspapers. It is now known that the association received a reply from the Ministry of Railways yesterday, saying: "The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce has read the telegram. All goods transported by railway are subject to responsible transportation fees. This is an established method of the Ministry that has been implemented for a long time. Coal catty cannot be unique, and when coal catty transportation was not handled responsibly, coal merchants had to hire their own escorts, and their wages and fares were not small. The theft and shortage of coal catty could still not be avoided. These losses were borne by the coal merchants. In addition, there may be various improper expenses, and the amount is far more than the ordinary responsible fee of 10%. Now that the railway is responsible for transportation, coal catty can be exempted from the above-mentioned various expenses, and in case of loss, the railway will compensate in full. Although coal merchants pay an additional 10% of the ordinary responsible fee, what they save is more than double. From the perspective of the railway itself, the reduction of coal catty freight rates over the years has already lost the transportation cost, but in order to maintain state coal, it is tolerated and implemented. Now, in order to ensure the safety and cost savings of state coal transportation, the implementation of responsible transportation increases anti-theft equipment, adds escort police, and prepares funds to compensate for losses. The additional 10% ordinary responsible fee is used to slightly compensate. The Coal Industry Association pointed out that it is a disguised price increase, which is ignorant of the gains and losses. The request to charge the old price for state coal truck transportation should not be discussed. I hope you will reply to the Coal Industry Association and inform all coal merchants. This is a special reply, Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu (seal)"

Revised Election of Directors and Supervisors: The Ministry of Internal Affairs instructed the Association, saying: "According to the investigation, the Ministry previously stipulated in the first half of Article 4 of the Regulations on the Administration of the Red Cross Society of the Republic of China (the Association shall have directors and supervisors, each with a certain number of people, who shall be elected from the representatives of the national members by the National Congress of Members) and Article 24, paragraph 2 of the Implementing Rules (the aforementioned directors shall be elected from the members by the National Congress of Members); Article 26, paragraph 2 of the same Implementing Rules also has the same provisions. By carefully examining the content of the articles, the scope of the qualifications for the election of directors and supervisors is different, and there is no ambiguity in application. The National Congress of Members of the Association is about to be convened, and it should be clearly interpreted as soon as possible to follow. Moreover, considering that the duties of the directors and supervisors of the Association are heavy, it is appropriate to widely solicit talents for the candidates in order to benefit the Association. It seems inappropriate to limit it to the representatives of the members and deprive the right of the majority of the members to be elected. The Executive Yuan has been requested to review and approve that the qualifications for the election of the directors and supervisors of the Association in this session shall still be handled in accordance with the provisions of the Implementing Rules. At the same time, in order to strive for consistency in the content of the regulations, the Legislative Yuan is also requested to consider revising the Administration Regulations for application in the volume. Hereby, the Executive Yuan instructed in the 177th meeting of the court, and the resolution (passed), and has been consulted to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation and amendment of the regulations. This is hereby instructed to be followed, and the qualifications for the election of the directors and supervisors of the Association in this session shall still be handled in accordance with the provisions of the Implementing Rules. This is a very important instruction."

Brief Record of the Disaster in Longquan, Zhejiang Province 117

The Chinese Jisheng Association recently received a telegram from Qian Desheng, Shao Zegui, and hundreds of other representatives of the disaster victims in Changan Town, Longquan, Zhejiang, saying that Changan Town, Longquan, has suffered from severe drought for three months in June, July, and August this year. The fields are cracked, and the rice is scorched. The farmers are drawing water day and night and are very anxious. On September 2, they suddenly suffered a bandit disaster. More than 5,000 people attacked the territory, kidnapped and looted, and searched every household. They were tied up and carried away day and night. The people fled and hid in the thickets. The dead are gone. The rich have emptied their pockets, and the poor have exhausted every drop, so that all the shops in the town are closed, and the smoke is cut off. Forty to fifty percent of them cannot make a fire. Now, although the bandits have retreated to the Fujian border, Changan is only forty miles away from the Fujian border. People are panicking, and they move several times a night. It is especially difficult to find food. Natural and man-made disasters are coming together, which is an unprecedented tragedy. Before and after Changan Town, the surrounding towns and villages such as Xiaomei and Chatian in Nanxiang, Tangshang and Xitou in Xixiang have also suffered the same disasters. Millions of people are clamoring and waiting to be fed urgently. They are crying and begging for rescue and relief to comfort the survivors. According to the records, the disaster in Zhejiang Province is extremely tragic, and other provinces are also unavoidable. The last surprising news from astronomers was that the typhoon also had a tendency to hit Shanghai. Fortunately, the wind changed direction and was exempted. It is enough to show that God loves the people of Shanghai, because there are always philanthropists in Shanghai, who have the heart to help people and benefit things, or design fundraising, generously donate, and work together to provide relief and eliminate disasters. The reason is that all those who have the idea of disaster relief will be blessed by God. The truth is not bad. I hope that enthusiastic colleagues will quickly show compassion, use kindness to eliminate fierceness, and provide as much assistance as possible to the compatriots in the disaster-stricken provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, and Hubei, so as to avoid the arrival of a disaster. The opportunity must not be lost. If everyone has a kind thought, it will surely spread peace to the earth.

Begging for Relief in Wangdian District, Jiaxing 118

Silkworm Failure and Rice and Bean Shortage, People Are Not Living

There are Several Cases of Robbing Rice and Sitting Down to Eat, Which Is Quite Worrying

Zhejiang Province suffered from severe drought this year, and the rivers, fields, and crops are dry everywhere. Wangdian Town in Jiaxing County along the Shanghai-Hangzhou Road is particularly affected. Special letters have been sent to various places to beg for relief. The disaster situation, losses, and disturbances caused by the disaster in the district are recorded as follows to show the urgency of waiting for relief.

Disaster Situation and Losses This Year: The total area of Wangdian District is 217,593 mu, 147,000 mu of which are fields, and 63,000 mu of which are land. Only 46,200 mu were planted, and few of them grew. According to accurate statistics, only 14,000 stone of rice can be harvested, and 219,800 stone were lost due to drought. The 63,000 mu of land are all mulberry gardens. The failure of silkworms is needless to say. The soybeans planted in the middle of the mulberry gardens are difficult to grow due to the long drought. It is estimated that only 3,000 stone can be harvested, and 23,000 stone were lost. The loss of only rice and beans is more than 1,751,400 yuan.

Process of Disturbances Caused by the Disaster: The large-scale rice grabbing on July 22 originated in Wangdian. By July 23, ruffians mixed in, and the momentum became even more turbulent. The entire town lost more than 600 stone of rice and beans. Although the police and security teams tried their best to suppress it, the government distributed accumulated grains, and local public groups presided over porridge to quell the turmoil, but it was like a drop in the bucket and difficult to be universal and lasting. Therefore, from July 25 to August 8, although the town appeared peaceful, in the ten days or so, according to the survey in the countryside, there were 40 cases of rice grabbing and sitting down to eat. Recently, even half of the savings are difficult to escape. There have been many reports of grabbing clothes and silver dollars. On July 25, on the way from this district to Xiashi, the crowd crowded on the railway for rice, and the opening of the district train was blocked. This phenomenon has never been seen in western Zhejiang, and it can also be seen that it is serious now.

Suzhou High Court Orders All Courts to Establish Appointed Defense Attorneys 119

Ten Provisional Regulations Specified

Jiangsu High Court sent Instruction No. 2380 to all Lawyers' Associations, stating: "Received Instruction No. 11892 from the Ministry of Judicial Administration. This court submitted a document proposing provisional regulations for the appointment of permanent public defenders by this court, requesting review and instructions. The document stated: (The document and regulations have been reviewed. Public defenders are appointed by the state, provided with a fixed salary, and are a type of public office dedicated to criminal defense, not concurrently held by lawyers. This is evident from foreign legal precedents and Article 8 of the Implementing Regulations of our country's Criminal Procedure Law. The original proposed regulations are no different from the previous practice of courts contracting with lawyers for appointment. They do not fully comply with the system of public defenders. The original proposed regulations should be changed to (Appointed Defense Attorneys). There are also points in the article on (Appointed Defense Attorneys) that should be revised, and the Ministry has made appropriate revisions and will issue a separate copy. You are to refer to this and prepare a corrected copy for submission to the Ministry for record. The regulations are retained. This is the order, etc.) In view of this, this court previously intended to appoint lawyers Liu Zutang, Tao Jianshan, Xu Zhu, and Liang Wei as permanent public defenders, which should now be changed to (Appointed Defense Attorneys). It is imperative to issue the revised regulations, instructing you to take note and forward them to the Lawyers' Association for compliance. This is the order. Enclosed is a copy of the Provisional Regulations for Appointed Defense Attorneys. (Article 1) For the sake of expediting criminal cases, this court appoints four lawyers to serve as designated defense counsel in cases where defense counsel is required by law. (Article 2) The aforementioned defense counsel shall be appointed by this court from among lawyers practicing in the area under its jurisdiction. (Article 3) The term of appointment for appointed defense counsel shall be six months, and a new appointment shall be made upon expiration. (Article 4) After the expiration of the term of appointment for appointed defense counsel, they must continue their duties until a successor takes over. (Article 5) Appointed defense counsel shall not be absent arbitrarily from scheduled hearings of cases for which they have been appointed. If they are unable to attend court on time due to a genuine reason, they shall first notify this court and entrust another lawyer to act as defense counsel. (Article 6) Appointed defense counsel shall not appoint another defense counsel for cases for which they have already been designated. (Article 7) Serving as appointed defense counsel is an obligation, but each lawyer may be given a monthly allowance of forty yuan, half of which shall be paid by this court, and the remainder shall be borne by the respective Lawyers' Associations. (Article 8) This court shall provide a separate office for appointed defense counsel to facilitate their work. (Article 9) If appointed defense counsel perform their duties diligently or achieve particularly excellent results during their term, the presiding judge of each court may report to the President of this court for appropriate rewards. Those who violate their duties shall be disciplined by the court president in accordance with the disciplinary procedures stipulated in the Lawyers' Regulations. (Article 10) These regulations shall take effect from the date of approval by the Ministry."

Memorial Service for Ms. Wu Yongmei 120

The remains of Wu Yongmei, a female student at the National Jinan University who was crushed to death, are still temporarily placed in the Chinese Funeral Home on Haig Road. Yesterday morning at 10:00 AM, the Jiangxi Alumni Association of the university and all the students, deeply saddened by Ms. Wu's cautious and intelligent nature, love of learning, early loss of parents, and suffering of hardship, feeling sympathy for her solitary life, held a memorial service to express their admiration. Details are recorded below:

Venue Arrangement: The memorial service was held in the Zhiyuan Hall of the university. A banner was hung above the entrance, reading "Memorial Service for the Late Ms. Wu Yongmei." Registration desks for guests and students were set up on both sides. Inside the hall, the national flag and the image of Ms. Wu were hung in the center, surrounded by wreaths and white cloth elegiac couplets. Over a thousand guests and students attended, all with solemn and sorrowful expressions. The university authorities also announced a one-hour suspension of classes to express their condolences. After the opening of the meeting, Shen Pengfei, the chief officiant, gave a report, stating that Ms. Wu was excellent in character and academics at the university, humble and amiable, and had extraordinary aspirations, always thinking of contributing to the country and society. It was unexpected that such an accident would occur, and she would die with hatred, truly a loss of talent for the country and a model for the students. Then, Meng Shouchun, the Dean of the Faculty of Arts, Zhang Yaoxiang, the Director of the Department of Education, and representatives of the Jiangxi Alumni Association of Jiaotong University successively spoke.

Ms. Wu's Life: Reported by Ms. Li Xiyong, stating that Ms. Wu was born in November of the second year of Xuantong. When she was four years old, her mother passed away, and she went to live with her grandmother. The following year, she was raised by her stepmother, Ms. Kong, who loved her as if she were her own daughter. She entered elementary school at the age of twelve and did not leave until she graduated from high school. She was diligent and cautious in her studies, and never spoke harshly to others. She always excelled in exams and was highly praised by teachers and friends. Unexpectedly, Ms. Wu lost her father at the age of sixteen and, as an orphan, raised her younger siblings, fulfilling her responsibilities as a child. In the summer of the 21st year, her stepmother arranged a marriage with the Min family. When Ms. Wu heard the news, the red thread had already been tied. Ms. Wu, known for her filial piety, did not dare to disobey her mother's wishes, but because the matter concerned her entire life, she appealed to her father's friend, Mr. Ping, to cancel the engagement. Although she achieved her wish, a rift had already formed between mother and daughter. In the summer of the previous year, she was admitted to Jinan University, majoring in education. She studied diligently but was often unhappy. Ms. Wu had experienced great changes and suffered hardships in her life. This summer, she returned to sweep her father's tomb, and before a month had passed, she was tragically devoured by a "city tiger". If her spirit is aware, she will forever hold resentment in the afterlife.

Aftermath: According to Mr. Cai Cixue, a representative of the Wu case support association, the support association decided to assist Ms. Wu's family in filing a lawsuit with the court, build a memorial碑 at the scene of the accident, and raise funds for a memorial educational essay award to commemorate her memory permanently and comfort her soul. Her nephew, Zhenheng, and niece, Zhenxian, are currently studying at the Wusong Merchant Marine School, and her cousin, Ping Zuren, works at Jiaoda University. They all expressed great grief and firmly requested that the court severely punish the murderer and provide preferential treatment to the deceased. As for Ms. Wu's remains, they will be transported back to her hometown for burial after the conclusion of the lawsuit.

Beijing-Shanghai Railway Issues 10-Trip and 20-Trip Tickets Between Shanghai-Wuxi Stations 121

Effective from October 10th

Valid for Two and Four Months

The Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, in order to facilitate passengers, has decided to issue two types of first, second, and third class multi-trip tickets, 10-trip and 20-trip, between the stations of North Shanghai, Nanxiang, Kunshan, Suzhou, and Wuxi on the Beijing-Shanghai line, starting from October 10th of this year. The 10-trip tickets are priced at 85% of the regular fare, with a validity of two months. The 20-trip tickets are priced at 70% of the regular fare, with a validity of four months. Passengers purchasing these tickets must submit two 6.5 square centimeter (i.e., one square inch) photos, one of which will be affixed to the ticket and the other kept at the station for reference. When boarding, passengers must first present the ticket to the ticket office to have it stamped with the date and train number. If the ticket is found to be unstamped on the train, the passenger must pay for the ticket according to regulations. Due to the separation of duties, the date stamp must be applied first, followed by the train number in the blank space. All issuing rules are summarized and printed on the inside cover of the ticket according to the passenger transport regulations attachment for passengers' reference. When issuing the aforementioned tickets at each station, the area on the ticket where the photo is affixed should also be stamped with the date stamp. When calculating the discounted fare for these tickets, fractions less than five cents should be rounded up to five cents, and fractions of five cents or more but less than ten cents should be rounded up to ten cents. The inspection, tearing, and collection of these tickets, and other related matters should be carefully noted by all relevant staff to avoid omissions.

A Tragic Brawl in Yinxiang Port 126

The Public Works Department Will Begin Free Vaccination 127

Starting from October 1st, the Public Works Department Health Department will begin free vaccination, which will be undertaken separately by the health sub-departments of each district and the vaccination vehicles. Factory owners who wish to vaccinate their workers can contact the nearest health sub-department to arrange a time. The vaccination time of each sub-department is from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM for Chinese people and from 4:00 PM to 5:00 PM for foreigners, except on Saturdays and Sundays. As for the vaccination vehicles, Vehicle No. 1 will be in the East First District every Monday, in the East Second District on Tuesday, in the East Third District on Wednesday morning, in the East Fourth and East Fifth Districts on Wednesday afternoon, in the North First and North Second Districts on Thursday, in the North Fourth District on Friday, and in the North Third District on Saturday. Vaccination Vehicle No. 2 will be in the West Fifth District every Monday, in the West Second District on Tuesday, in the West Third District on Wednesday, in the West Fourth District on Thursday, in the Central First District on Friday morning, in the Central Second District on Friday afternoon, and in the Central Third District on Saturday. The addresses and telephone numbers of the health sub-departments in each district are listed below: East 1: 30 Songpan Road, 50691; East 2: 311 Yangzhou Road, 50271; East 3: 67 Huade Road, 51071; East 4 and East 5: 10 Tongzhou Road, 52773; North 1 and North 2: 130 Haining Road, 43035; North 3: 190A North Sichuan Road, 46776; North 4: 270 North Fujian Road, 40277; West 1: 260 Avenue Road, 30447; West 2: 160 Maigen Road, 30449; West 3: 435 Roberts Road, 31076; West 4: 1360 Yuyuan Road, 27346; Central 1 and Central 2: 667 Fuzhou Road, 91574; Central 3: 340 Hankou Road, 90273.

Mr. Ha Shao Fu Passed Away Yesterday Morning 128

Mr. Ha Shao Fu, a respected elder of the Muslim community, passed away at his residence in Shanghai yesterday morning at the age of 79. Mr. Ha was charitable throughout his life and served as the chairman of the Shanghai Qingzhen (Mosque) Board of Directors. He did much for the Muslim charitable cause, and also enthusiastically supported non-Muslim charitable works, serving as a member of the Red Cross Society and a director of the Shanghai Shangxian Hall. His death at such an old age has been deeply mourned by all who knew him.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Releases Shanghai Commercial Practices 129

The Shanghai Commercial Practices compiled by Yan E'sheng, Secretary of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, is a reference book for resolving commercial disputes and legal questions. The selected materials are all good customs of the Shanghai market, totaling more than 180 items, divided into 22 categories. Those belonging to industries are most detailed for money houses, woolen cloth, piece goods, silk satin, hardware, insurance, and various Chinese and foreign transactions. Those belonging to categories are most complete for bills, sales, orders, partnerships, and partner events. At the end of the book, there are 42 kinds of industry rules, which are particularly important. Since its publication, it has been praised by all sectors of the country. Even the business circles in Yunnan, Guizhou, Chahar, Suiyuan, Shaanxi, and Gansu provinces have sent letters to order it. The book is published by Shanghai Xinsheng News Agency, with a thick volume, and sells for 1.5 yuan (plus one yuan for mail orders). Now, to facilitate the purchase by the judicial and business circles of all provinces and cities, the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Dispatch Office is specially entrusted to issue it on behalf of the Chamber of Commerce.

Surtax on Cars Still Collected as Usual 130

Recently, there was a report that the approved Shanghai local budget had an order to reduce the surtax on car donations. The reporter specially visited the financial authorities to inquire about the collection of this surtax. They were answered that the name of this surtax is "Surtax on Interconnected Cars in Five Provinces and Cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Beijing, and Shanghai." It is based on Article 4 of the Provisional Regulations on Interconnected Cars in Five Provinces and Cities, which stipulates that 10% of the car donation should be collected and submitted to the National Economic Commission and the Five Provinces and Cities Transportation Commission jointly organized by the five provinces and cities, for the purpose of handling all equipment on the public roads of the five provinces. Therefore, the surtax is a collection in lieu and not an ordinary city revenue. Whether it will be reduced in the future will depend on the decision of the National Economic Commission and the five provinces and cities. Before the decision to reduce it is made, the city will continue to collect it as usual.

Serious Disaster in Jiangpu 131

Representatives Sent to Shanghai to Raise Relief Funds

Jiangpu County faces the capital across the water. The whole territory is divided into five districts, covering more than 300,000 mu of land, of which 80-90% are mountainous land and only 10-20% are enclosed fields. The rural economy has not yet recovered from the severe flooding of the year before last. This year's severe drought has turned into a scene of misery everywhere. The county has always been known as a poor and sick township, and the poor harvest this year is normal. In addition, the natural environment is not as good as that of the five southern counties. The people of the whole county, in addition to working hard to cultivate self-sufficiency, have no other side industries to adjust. Unexpectedly, since the beginning of spring, there has been little rainfall, and locusts have wreaked havoc. Fortunately, they were put out early to avoid disaster. Since the beginning of summer, there has been no rain, the land has cracked, and the seedlings have withered. The scene is desolate, as if one has climbed to barren land. Cries are everywhere, and there is no way to seek help. Although the various charitable organizations in the county have organized a famine relief association to carry out emergency relief, the local economy is strained, and they are exhausted. Moreover, as the cold winter is approaching, the famine relief work is urgent. Therefore, they have sent a representative, Mr. Lin Chunting, to Shanghai to appeal for help. It is reported that Mr. Lin arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday and is now contacting the various charitable organizations separately.
