Xiong Guohua Assassinated in His Hospital Bed

Police Detective and Patrolman Also Killed Tragically

丨The Murderer Escaped, The Situation is Serious丨

At 11:35 PM on the 16th of this month, an assassination occurred in Room 34 of the Shenji Qianji Hotel, No. 37 Huajin Lane, Simalu Road. The victim was named Xiong Guohua, said to be from Taizhou, 34 years old. At the time, it was reported that his injuries were not serious, so after being sent to Renji Hospital on Shandong Road for treatment, he gradually recovered. The details have been reported in this newspaper. However, yesterday afternoon, he was shot and killed in the hospital, and a detective and a patrolman were also killed. The details are recorded below:

Xiong Guohua Recovering Well On the evening of the 16th of this month, Xiong Guohua was in Room 34 of the Qianji Hotel when two bandits tricked him into opening the door and shot him. He fell to the ground unconscious. The hotel accountant immediately reported to the police, who immediately dispatched Chinese and Western detectives to investigate. Xiong Guohua was sent to Renji Hospital on Shandong Road for treatment. He was sent to Bed No. 18 in Ward No. 145 on the first floor. After examination by the doctor, it was found that he had three injuries, one in the mouth, one at the root of the neck, and one in the right chest. However, none were serious. After the bullets were removed and he was carefully treated, his injuries gradually recovered, and he would soon be discharged from the hospital. However, at that time, the police, because the criminals in this case had not been caught, and Xiong's whereabouts were also suspicious, specially assigned three detectives to take turns guarding the hospital every day to prevent accidents.

Drawing Guns Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 PM,

Pretending to Visit Renji Hospital opened its doors because it was the designated visiting time. Visitors entered one after another. However, in order to prevent irrelevant people from entering, the hospital issued a visitor's pass. However, at about 3:40 PM, four more men came, two wearing Zhongshan suits, one wearing a black long gown, and one wearing a blue cloth long gown, about 20 or 30 years old. They went to the hospital and broke in. At that time, the person checking the passes at the door of the accounting room asked them for passes. The four men ignored him and went straight in. The pass checker stopped them because they violated the regulations. While they were arguing, the four men each pulled out a gun and showed it to the pass checker, saying, "This is the ticket." Then, two men escorted him back into the accounting room and guarded the staff in the telephone room, preventing them from moving. At the same time, they blocked the telephone and cut off communication.

Hit by Two Bullets At this time, two men went

Died Instantly straight to Ward No. 145 on the first floor and broke into the room. Xiong Guohua was still lying in bed at Bed No. 28. Suddenly, he saw someone entering and was about to ask a question when the two men pulled out guns and each fired a shot at him, both in the head and brain. Xiong was caught off guard and was unable to resist because he had just recovered from his injuries. He was killed without resistance. Blood and brains splattered all over the bed. Seeing that their goal had been achieved, the two men turned around and fled. At that time, the patients in the next room suddenly heard gunshots and were frightened. The other staff members were unable to capture them, so they had to let them run down the stone stairs and escape.

Fan Yongquan At this time, Fan Yongquan, No. 253 detective

Died Tragically from the Laozao Police Station, Qingjiang, who was responsible for monitoring Xiong Guohua, happened to be sitting idly in the reception room downstairs. Suddenly, he heard gunshots from Ward No. 145 and knew something was wrong. He quickly pulled out his pistol and walked out of the reception room. But at this time, the two murderers had already run to the side of the small garden downstairs and met up with the two men in the accounting room. Fan thought they were escaping from upstairs, so he didn't suspect anything and walked towards the men. However, his weapon had already been seen by them. The holder was unintentional, but the viewer was intentional. They thought that Fan had seen through their actions, so they pointed their guns at Fan and shouted for him to stop and raise his hands. Fan was caught off guard and unable to resist, so he had to raise his hands. However, in a flash, heartless bullets were fired like a string of beads, hitting Fan in the chest. He fell to the ground in response, blood gushing out, and died instantly.

A Patrolman But the disaster unexpectedly

Died Accidentally Happened. While Detective Fan was being killed and the murderers had not yet escaped from the hospital, a fight broke out at the French Concession Police Station. The injured person was named Yang Yulin, but his injuries were very minor, so he ordered Patrolman No. 721 to escort him to Renji Hospital for treatment. After entering the door, Yang Yulin walked alone past the small garden to the clinic for treatment, with the French Concession patrolman following behind, about ten yards away. The murderers saw him and thought he was there to arrest them, so they rushed forward and shouted at the French Concession patrolman to stop. The French Concession patrolman No. 721 knew that the situation was not good. Moreover, he was empty-handed and unable to resist, so he quickly turned around to escape. However, the four murderers fired three shots from behind, all hitting him, penetrating his chest. He also fell to the side of the small garden and died. After killing three people, the four murderers were like entering a no-man's land. They calmly escaped from the hospital and fled in different directions. When the police received the report and rushed a full team of Chinese and Western armed detectives to pursue them, they had long since disappeared. They quickly notified the French Concession Police Station to first send the body of Chinese patrolman No. 721 to the coroner's office. In the evening, they continued to send the bodies of Fan and Xiong to the coroner's office to await the court's examination this morning. They also notified the city's police agencies to provide assistance in arresting the escaped murderers.

Wu Hua Bank Depositors File Lawsuit 134

Deputy Managers Fan Shaoliang, Wang Jian'e, and Eight Others Named as Defendants

Depositors List Three Major Counts of Fraud and Breach of Trust, Detailing Events Before and After

丨Plaintiffs and Others Absent From Yesterday's Trial丨

The Guangzhou Wu Hua Industrial Trust Bank established a Shanghai branch at No. 130 Ningbo Road in the Shanghai International Settlement around October of last year. By June of this year, the branch had opened a sub-branch at the intersection of Avenue Dubail and Avenue Joffre in the French Concession's Eight Immortals Bridge area. Unexpectedly, on August 21, both the branch and sub-branch suddenly went bankrupt simultaneously. Due to clearing issues, the head office and the branch argued, each hiring lawyers to publish accusations in newspapers, engaging in heated debates. Currently, ten creditors holding savings and current account deposits in the branch and sub-branch – Chu Longgen, Chen Xianji, Luo Lihua (female), Shi Pengfei, Du Zhiji, Shi Bilong, Shen Peng, Zhou Delin, Wang Fulin, Pan Yuanji, and others – have jointly retained four lawyers, Zhang Shijie, Lou Yunmei, Xu Jie, and Mao Fengwu, to file a criminal complaint with the First Special District Court. They accuse Fan Shaoliang and Ye Haitian, deputy managers of the Wu Hua Industrial Trust Bank Shanghai Branch, Wang Jian'e and Wu Yousan, deputy managers of the Wu Hua Industrial Trust Bank Shanghai Eight Immortals Bridge Sub-branch, as well as Xie Shunzhi, Tang Songshan, Tang Shoumin, and Chen Bingqian, managers and advisors of the branch, of fraud and breach of trust, requesting legal judgment and sentencing.

The substance of the complaint states: "Regarding the matter of fraud and breach of trust, requesting legal judgment and sentencing, the plaintiffs are depositors of the now-bankrupt Wu Hua Industrial Trust Bank Shanghai Branch and Eight Immortals Bridge Sub-branch. The defendants are the business operators of the branch and sub-branch. According to regulations, the establishment of bank branches must be approved by the Ministry of Finance before commencing operations. The Wu Hua branch and sub-branch in Shanghai were established without the approval of the Ministry of Finance. Therefore, the branch and sub-branch did not meet the substantive requirements for establishment, and the act of accepting cash deposits was undoubtedly an illegal act. Even if they claim to have registered with a foreign government, conducting business within Chinese territory without legal approval should not qualify them as legal entities. All actors should bear their responsibilities. The defendants are all important officers of the Wu Hua branch and sub-branch. Having discovered illegal activities, the plaintiffs are entitled to file a complaint against them. The facts of defrauding money and breaching trust are described below: (1) The Wu Hua Bank Shanghai Branch was established in October of last year at No. 130 Ningbo Road. By late June of this year, the Eight Immortals Bridge Sub-branch was established at Nos. 126 to 168 Avenue Dubail. According to recent reports about the inside story of the bank, it was already struggling to support itself.

Expanding Empty Ventures to Absorb Cash to Maintain Lavish Decoration, Further Utilizing Advertising Propaganda: Requiring Only Fifty Silver Dollars for Deposit, Without Guarantee, to Receive a Checkbook for Use in Society, Truly Opening Up an Unprecedented Special Case in Shanghai's Banking Industry. Furthermore, they cleverly established names such as "Five-Year Savings Plan," "Ten-Year Savings Plan," and "New Life Savings," using attractive interest rates in advertisements as bait. Unexpectedly, the branch went bankrupt in less than a year, and the sub-branch in only two months, simultaneously. The plaintiffs' trusted Five-Year Plan and Ten-Year Plan funds had already been paid monthly, but the defendants violated the five-year and ten-year missions, suddenly ceasing operations, causing the depositors' paid amounts to become the illegal property of the defendants or some of them. At the same time, depositors suffered damages, indicating that the initial (see advertisements in various newspapers on June 21 of this year when the bank opened) and the Five-Year and Ten-Year Plan and other high-interest savings regulations were all tools to absorb cash and obtain illegal profits. The defendants committed the crime of breach of trust under Article 366 of the Criminal Code. (2) The Wu Hua Bank Eight Immortals Bridge Sub-branch went bankrupt on August 21 of this year.

The Night Before, the Defendants Hired Two Automobiles to Secretly Transport the Savings of the Plaintiffs, Namely the Depositors, and Valuables Overnight to North Sichuan Road to Hide Them (see reports in various newspapers). After being discovered, a bookkeeper named Qu was unable to escape and was arrested by the French police and released on bail. It is verifiable. According to a statement published by Wang Jian'e, the manager of the defendant bank, in the newspaper on the 25th of this month, the sub-branch received a total of over 80,000 silver dollars in deposits, showing that the defendants had premeditated an organized fraud. As soon as they absorbed the deposits, they moved them to their private residences for enjoyment, which is very clear. The plaintiffs mistakenly believed in their five-year and ten-year long-term plans, sparing no effort to scrape together money from their hard work and handing it all over. Who knew that their advertisements and regulations were all fraudulent tricks? The defendants committed the crime of fraud under Article 363 of the Criminal Code. (3) According to Article 2 of the Savings Bank Law promulgated and implemented by the National Government on July 4, 1934, savings banks may not be established without the approval of the Ministry of Finance. Ordinary banks

Simultaneously Operating Savings Bank Business Must Collect Paid-Up Capital of at Least One Million National Currency. The bank organized by the defendants was not approved by the Ministry of Finance, and its capital, including the branch and sub-branch, did not reach 500,000 silver dollars (as reported in various newspapers on the 25th of this month). Therefore, it fundamentally could not simultaneously operate a savings business. Even if the law was promulgated and implemented on July 4 of this year, their previous actions would not be subject to sanctions. However, after the law was promulgated and implemented, they should no longer accept deposits from the plaintiffs. This is their violation of Article 2 of the law, which should be subject to the penalties of Article 16, Paragraph 1, also. Furthermore, Article 7 of the law lists regulations for the use of funds. According to a statement by Wang Jian'e, manager of the Wu Hua Bank Eight Immortals Bridge Sub-branch, published in the newspaper on the 25th of this month, the sub-branch's total deposit income was over 80,000 silver dollars, most of which was remitted to the branch. This is their violation of the use of funds, which, according to Articles 7 and 9 of the law, should be subject to the penalties of Article 16 of the same law, also. In summary, the defendants are all managers,

Important Officers of the Wu Hua Industrial Trust Bank Shanghai Branch and Eight Immortals Bridge Sub-branch. Based on the advertisements with text and pictures displayed by the Eight Immortals Bridge Sub-branch beforehand, deceiving the public, and the means of deliberately offering high interest rates to lure deposits, and the earlier actions of moving assets and documents before closing down and fleeing, it is reliable evidence that it was an organized fraud. Therefore, a complaint is specially filed in accordance with the law, begging for investigation, summoning the defendants for interrogation to clarify the facts, and imposing criminal penalties and fines according to law." The court verified the complaint and summoned the plaintiffs yesterday. The plaintiffs all arrived with their lawyers, but none of the defendants arrived. Lawyers arrived on their behalf. Presiding Judge Zhang Pengzu and Clerk Zheng Rong opened the second court for trial. First, the plaintiffs reported the amount of deposits lost, with the largest being 3,000 silver dollars and the smallest being 20 silver dollars. They also stated that the defendants opened the bank, using five-year and ten-year plans to absorb deposits and savings, and went bankrupt without reason in less than three months, which was indeed a fraudulent act. They requested the recovery of the lost deposits and savings, and requested punishment to deter future offenders. Then, Hua Maosheng, the defending lawyer for the first and second defendants, Fan Shaoliang and Ye Haitian, stated, "My clients saw the notice of today's hearing in the newspaper, but the summons

Was Delivered After Multiple Transfers and Has Not Yet Been Received, So They Did Not Appear. However, the Wu Hua Bank Branch is located at No. 130 Ningbo Road in the British Concession. Based on the issue of jurisdiction, we request a ruling and determination at the next hearing." The judge then instructed the plaintiffs that the addresses of the defendants on the complaint were provided by accountant Wang Sisui. Today, a copy of the complaint will be delivered in court, and a copy will be issued to each defendant's lawyer. Zheng Wenkai, the defending lawyer for the third defendant, Wang Jian'e, stated, "My client went to Nanjing on business and could not appear. My lawyer was appointed by his family. The defendant himself can appear at the next hearing." Ma Chang, representing the fourth defendant, Wu Yousan, stated, "My client is ill and can appear at the next hearing." Yuan Xingyun, representing the fifth, sixth, and seventh defendants, Xie Shunzhi, Tang Songshan, and Tang Shoumin, stated, "Tang Shoumin is absent due to illness. The others did not appear because they did not receive the summons." Yang Guoshu, representing the eighth defendant, Chen Bingqian, stated, "My client is 70 years old and is currently recuperating in Moganshan. The summons has been sent to him and he can appear at the next hearing." Finally, the plaintiffs' representing lawyers Zhang Shijie, Lou Yunmei, and Xu Jie supplemented their opinions and submitted a copy of the Ministry of Finance's disapproval. The court reviewed the statements and instructed that a date be set for another summons, and then adjourned.

The police rushed to the scene, and both sides exchanged gunfire. The Western police fired a total of six shots, and the two Chinese police fired a total of six shots. The bandits fired back continuously like machine guns. As a result of the battle, the Western police suffered leg injuries in one place each and fell to the ground in pain. Zhang Guixiang and Zhou Caixiang, two of the bandits, were shot in the legs. Zhang fell to the ground on the spot and was captured. Zhou was very fierce and fled despite his injuries. The other two bandits also disappeared during the chaos. At this time, the Jing'an Temple police station had received a report, and the police chief immediately dispatched all Chinese and Western detectives, armed, to conduct a siege. While passing by Avenue Kénéral Liéautey, Zhou was getting into a rickshaw to escape, and was intercepted by the detectives. A pistol and seven bullets were found on his person, and he was brought back to the police station along with Zhang. The injured Western police were sent to Hong'en Hospital for treatment. The two bandits confessed at the police station that there were a total of four of them. The ringleader had ordered them to go to the Cathay Hotel on Avenue Joffre. Upon arriving there, the ringleader sent them to Dapu Bridge in the French Concession, where someone handed them three pistols and instructed them to accept them immediately. The firearms were to be transported back to Jiangbei, and if they encountered interrogation on the way, they could open fire and resist arrest. They stated that they had obtained the pistols on the orders of the ringleader and opened fire because they were being investigated by the patrol police. The police station still needs to investigate whether these confessions are false. However, the two bandits are seriously injured and have been sent to the Municipal Council Hospital for treatment. Chen Qiao'lai (21 years old), a small sister of Hong's from Anhui, worked as a prostitute at No. 4 Weichang Lane on East/West Seward Road. Knowing that something had happened, she immediately checked and found that several pieces of gold jewelry and 50 silver dollars were missing. Other items were untouched. Forcibly Kidnapping Son, Hiding Him, Forcing Him to Write Letter to Father for Extortion 137

The Reason is That the Engagement Used the Concubine's Name

Out of Resentment, Zhao Lu's did This Illegal Act

Wen, the legal wife of Zhao Zengfu, the owner of the Zhao He Xing fruit store in Xinjie, Minhang Town in the southwest of this county, passed away many years ago, leaving behind a son named Ziwen (currently 21 years old), who was working as a typesetter in the Lisheng Chang Printing Office in Shengze. In the 11th year of the Republic (1922), Zhao Zengfu, lacking someone to care for the family, remarried Lu of this town as his stepmother through matchmaking. At that time, Ziwen was only nine years old, and Lu raised him, treating him with exceptional affection, as if he were her own child. However, Zhao Zengfu was fond of women, so in the 16th year of the Republic (1927), he became involved with a woman. Soon after, he had an affair with Yang A'er, a young woman from this town. He favored the new and abandoned the old, and also neglected Lu. Therefore, Lu often argued with Zhao Zengfu, and they were incompatible. Before long, Zhao became involved with a woman named Yan. Because he could not stand Lu's harassment, he took money and left home in the 20th year of the Republic (1931) and lived with Yan at No. 11 Sanjiaodi, Xujiahui. Zhao Zengfu, because his son had grown up, asked a matchmaker to arrange a marriage for Ziwen with a woman named Zheng Wanping from Shengze. They chose to get married on the 19th of this month and sent out invitations to relatives and friends in advance. However, Lu felt that she had raised Ziwen for many years, and the invitations were printed with the name of a concubine, so out of resentment, she invited Li Zhongda, Jin Xiang, and others to Shanghai and opened Room 21 at the Central Hotel at Xiaodongmen. She also invited Yao Jinyuan, a shareholder of the Xieshun Restaurant in Yuhangqiao, and others, and at 8:00 a.m. on the 10th of this month, hired a car to go to Zhao Zengfu's house in Sanjiaodi, Xujiahui, and forcibly dragged Zhao Ziwen into the car and hid him in Room 21 of the Central Hotel. Later, they moved him to Room 12 and forced Ziwen to write a letter to his father, Zhao Zengfu, telling him to come to the Central Hotel for negotiations. If Zhao Zengfu was afraid and did not come, then Ziwen would have to issue an IOU for 700 yuan to repay Lu's debts. However, Zhao Zengfu was working as an accountant at the Jinghua Leather Industrial Cooperative in the French Concession. The letter written by Ziwen was sent to the cooperative by Jin Xiang, dispatched by Lu. Because Zhao was out, a colleague at the cooperative sent the letter to Zhao's elder brother, Zhao Zengxiang, who opened the letter and was shocked. He believed that Lu's actions were akin to kidnapping, so he rushed to the hotel to contact them. However, Lu and others had already moved elsewhere. Zhao Zengxiang was extremely anxious, fearing that his nephew Ziwen would suffer a tragic accident. He immediately asked lawyer Pan Zhensheng to write a letter to the Second Branch of the First District, requesting the police to rush to the scene. As a result, Ziwen was rescued in Room 12, and Lu, Jin Xiang, Li Zhongda, and Li's mother, Pei, were arrested on the spot. Later, Yao Jinyuan, Xu Shunsheng, and others were also arrested and sent to the Third Section, and then transferred to the District Court. Yesterday afternoon, Presiding Judge Shao Qinzhi specially opened the Third Court for trial. The plaintiff Zhao Zengfu retained lawyer Pan Zhensheng to appear in court and requested an incidental private prosecution, requesting compensation for all losses. After the judge took the bench, he ordered Lu, who was in custody, to be brought to court. She confessed that she was 47 years old, from Minhang, and opened the Lu Shunxing fruit store in Minhang. Her husband, Zhao Zengfu, married her in the 11th year of the Republic (1922), and they separated in the 20th year (1931). Her son Ziwen was born to the former wife and is now working in the printing industry in Shengze. On the first day of August of this year, I came to Shanghai to look for my husband Zhao Zengfu but did not find him, so I brought Ziwen to the hotel. The letter was written by Ziwen at my direction. The judge asked how many of you went to Xujiahui in a car. She answered that she, Li Zhongda, Yao Jinyuan, and three others went. Li Zhongda confessed that he was 28 years old, from Minhang, and was a distant relative of Lu's. This time, he accompanied Lu to Xujiahui in a car and brought Zhao Ziwen to the hotel. They are mother and son and this was not kidnapping. Please investigate. Yao Jinyuan confessed that he and Lu and others went to Zhao Zengfu's house in Xujiahui and took Zhao Ziwen to the hotel, which was true. However, he did not know about the letter. The plaintiff Zhao Zengfu confessed that he was involved with Lu in the 11th year of the Republic (1922) and separated from each other in the 21st year (1932). On the morning of September 9th, Lu hired a car and kidnapped my son. Their purpose was for money. Please punish them. Zhao Ziwen confessed that Lu was his stepmother three years ago. I worked in the printing industry in Shengze. On the morning of the ninth of this month, they dragged me to the hotel and ordered me to write a letter, telling my father to come for negotiations. Their intention of detaining me privately was to get money. They also forced me to write an IOU for 700 yuan, but I refused, so I did not write it. The judge asked and concluded and requested Prosecutor Tang to come to court to present his arguments once. The judge, with the case already clear, considered it concluded. Lawyer Pan rose and said that the plaintiff's incidental private prosecution requested compensation for losses and intended to file a separate lawsuit after the criminal judgment. The judge approved, and instructed that the case would be sentenced at 2:00 p.m. on the 29th of this month. The three defendants, Lu and other men and women, were returned to custody to await instructions.

Two Assassination Case Criminals Appeal, Case Returned for Retrial 139

Previously Committed Manslaughter of Jin Shoupei and Assassination of Wang Bin

Liu Guobao, a young man from Sichuan, and Li Decai, a man from Henan, both participated in a rebellion. In the summer of the previous year, they assassinated Cao Qingcheng, a supervisor of the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau from Hubei, at the mouth of Yuancheng Lane on Route Lafayette in the French Concession, killing him. At the same time, they mistakenly killed Jin Shoupei, a native of Baoshan, due to mistaken identity. Liu and Li were chased and captured on the spot by detectives, who seized a pistol and bullets. They were brought to the police station. Later, it was found that the assassination of Wang Bin, a supervisor of the investigation team of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters from Suzhou, in front of the Guosi Temple on Avenue Vilmorin, was also committed by Liu and others. Because they were political case murderers, they were transferred to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The police department filed a public prosecution in accordance with the law. As a result of the trial, Liu and Li were sentenced for the crime of rebellion and each was sentenced to imprisonment. In addition, they were each sentenced to death for the crime of murder, as reported in previous newspapers. Later, because the two criminals were dissatisfied with the judgment, they filed a petition with the original trial court to appeal to the Nanjing Supreme Court. The Supreme Court reviewed the entire case file and ruled that there were still doubts in the case and a detailed investigation was necessary. Therefore, the Supreme Court ruled to revoke the original trial judgment and return the case to the Third Branch of the High Court for retrial. It is now heard that the Third Branch of the High Court has received the case file and will soon open a court session to summon witnesses for investigation.

Marriage Dispute Arising from Opening a Butcher Shop Leads to Litigation 143

Yao Huifang, a native woman only twenty-two years of age, residing at 20, Lane 58, Xiaoshadu Road, received a middle-school education and is quite literate. Last year, through a matchmaker, she became engaged to Zhao Jingen, who resides at 15, Lane 186, Shanhai Guan Road. They held their wedding on November 13 of the same year. The couple's relationship was quite affectionate. However, Zhao's father passed away early, leaving only a stepmother, who did not care for Zhao because he was not her biological son. She let Zhao Jingen remain unemployed and did not help him find a job. Yao, seeing that her husband's continued idleness was not a sustainable long-term plan, obtained her mother's consent and opened a butcher shop, entrusting Zhao to manage it. However, Zhao was unwilling, and a rift developed in the couple's affection. Yao was subjected to cold remarks and ridicule and was falsely accused of infidelity. On the 25th of last month, he even confined her to the room and restricted her freedom. Later, Yao's mother reported to the police, who dispatched officers to release Yao. Yao, feeling that she could no longer live with such abuse, hired lawyers Cao Lin and Gu Hanli to file a separate residence lawsuit against Zhao in the First Special District Court, requesting a monthly payment of one hundred yuan, for a period of three years, totaling three thousand six hundred yuan, and to bear the litigation costs. The First Special District Court approved the request, and Judge Yu Changzi summoned Zhao Jingen in the 14th Civil Court yesterday morning. Zhao Jingen did not appear but retained lawyer Chen Bingxing as his representative. Yao Huifang also did not appear in court but was represented by her lawyer, who stated the reasons for the lawsuit. According to lawyer Chen's defense on behalf of Zhao, Zhao is an honest and taciturn man, and his relationship with the plaintiff has always been harmonious, with no mistreatment whatsoever, as known to the neighbors. The plaintiff's assertion of mistreatment is unfounded. As for the plaintiff's claim that he refused to manage the butcher shop, the defendant is not skilled in the butcher shop business and therefore cannot manage it. Furthermore, on the 23rd of last month, the plaintiff left for Ningbo on the pretext, and the defendant did not pay attention. Unexpectedly, the plaintiff's mother suddenly sent someone to look for the plaintiff. The defendant told them that she had returned to Ningbo yesterday, so why were they looking for her today? There must be a reason. He then secretly searched but could not find her. She did not return until late that night. Upon learning that the plaintiff was a young woman who did not return late at night, and suspecting her actions, he questioned her. The plaintiff was evasive, and the defendant did not want to publicize the family scandal, so he did not investigate further. On the 25th, the plaintiff's father, Yao Xingquan, came to advise his daughter, asking if she still wanted to eat in the Zhao family. After three hours, she finally replied that she wanted to eat. Unexpectedly, that evening, her mother reported to the police that he was obstructing her freedom. He was ashamed and angry and used this as an outlet, which is obvious. Now, the defendant is filing a counterclaim, demanding that the plaintiff fulfill her cohabitation obligations. As for the plaintiff's request for alimony, the defendant is not wealthy and cannot afford it. The plaintiff's lawsuit should be dismissed. Judge Yu, after reviewing the report, granted permission for the trial to proceed in the absence of both the plaintiff and defendant and rescheduled the hearing for October 8. At that time, both parties must appear in person, so that the court can mediate a settlement and avoid extremes that would harm their relationship.

Reading Q&A 158

Is it Necessary to Understand Natural Science Before Studying Social Science?

Answer to Xu Si

Mr. Xu wrote a letter saying that he saw an article, stating: "Natural science occurred first, and social science was established later. Therefore, speaking about social science without a foundation in natural science is simply metaphysics... Little does he know that the theoretical foundations of social science all come from natural science. If one does not even understand the basic knowledge of natural science, how can one understand social science?" Mr. Xu, because his knowledge of natural science is very shallow, doubted whether he had the qualifications to study natural science after reading this passage. Now, let's first answer his doubts!

"Natural science occurred first, and social science was established later." This is true. True social science has only existed for the past few decades, while natural science sprouted more than two thousand years ago. However, the chronological order of occurrence does not prove that social science grew directly from the foundation of natural science. Of course, we cannot deny that natural science and social science have a certain relationship. Many laws in social science must be explained with the help of natural science knowledge, but social phenomena are ultimately social phenomena, fundamentally different from natural phenomena. All laws of social development and changes in natural phenomena cannot be regarded as the same thing. If we overemphasize natural science when explaining social phenomena, we will fall into error. For example, using sexuality in jurisprudence to explain social phenomena, saying that the demise of a country was due to the struggle for a woman, using geography to explain human society, saying that the strength of the ancient north was due to the cold climate, etc., are all errors in explaining social phenomena with natural phenomena. Because the real reason for the demise of a country is that its economic power is insufficient to resist foreign invaders, and the strength of the ancient northerners is due to the difficult economic situation of their nomadic life. Social phenomena have their own laws, and this point must be clearly recognized first. (To be continued)

Shenbao National Goods Weekly

National Goods Discussion

An Advocacy for Women Using National Products from the National Products Society 160

— Ms. Chen Xuezhi

More than half of the Women's National Products Year has passed. We will temporarily put aside discussing the achievements of the past six months and focus on how we should truly strive in the work of the coming months!

The newspapers reported the day before yesterday that the Women's National Products Year Movement Committee held a joint meeting of the Economic Affairs Committee and the Third Committee to discuss the outline of the work for the second half of the year. Although some newspapers are launching a general attack on the committee and our women, I always feel that doing national products work is better than not doing it. Frankly speaking, the work of the Women's National Products Year Movement Committee in the first half of the year can be considered diligent! It would be too much to put the responsibility for this alarming trade deficit entirely on the shoulders of our women! The trade deficit has its own complex reasons, which are truly beyond our ability to eliminate. However, we still have to work hard and must not be discouraged by this!

It is naturally difficult to see immediate results from any endeavor, but the impact on the future is significant. Doing national products work is no different. Therefore, as long as we bury our heads and work hard, the effects will naturally be revealed in our present!

Now is truly the time to begin the work for the second half of the Women's National Products Year. Because I am also a member of the women's community, I will not hide my inadequacy and offer some suggestions. I wonder if the committee will be able to adopt them?

When we do something, we always hope it will have some practical value. Therefore, I feel that we should urgently organize a Women's National Products Society. On the one hand, it is practical, and on the other hand, it can serve as a permanent memorial to the Women's National Products Year. I have written down some key points for organizing the Women's National Products Society below:

(1) The purpose is to promote national products, develop the national economy, and cultivate the habit of using national products.

(2) There are no restrictions on membership qualifications; everyone is welcome to join.

(3) Members shall not purchase or use foreign goods except for necessities for which there are no national product substitutes.

(4) All members must undertake the following tasks:

(A) Introduce compatriots to join the society.

(B) Promote national products.

(C) Investigate the names, trademarks, and manufacturers of national products.

(D) Organize national product stores.

(E) Organize branch societies anytime, anywhere.

This Women's National Products Society of my dreams can be large or small. It can be as large as establishing various institutions to promote national products and the China National Products Company, or as small as two or three friends joining together to agree to use national products consistently. My hope is that everyone will do a little to develop the national economy to the best of their ability, especially the intellectuals who have already awakened. They should take the lead because they can clearly see the poisonous strategies of foreign goods dumping. They should take on the responsibility of awakening those who are not yet aware and work hard!

Contribution Talk

Autumn Has Arrived 161

— Editor

Autumn has arrived, and people's needs for clothing, food, and shelter will naturally require a change of environment. If readers don't believe it, try going to various national product companies and stores to see the shoulder-to-shoulder crowds, the hair ornaments and fragrant clothes, and the people coming and going are all purchasing autumn supplies, especially the housewives in charge of household affairs. During this Women's National Products Year, it is truly the most modern and appropriate thing for women to purchase national products. Therefore, some people say that China's future does indeed have some glimmer of hope. Despite the Japanese promoting their goods, establishing Japanese goods markets everywhere, and unscrupulous merchants selling Japanese goods, no one with a level of knowledge above the horizon does not want to use national products, handle national products, and believe in national products. It can be seen that the promotion of national products in the future will be relatively more convenient. However, as people's hearts are deteriorating and there is too much counterfeiting, the patriotic women and young ladies who happily use national products should pay attention to the following four points:

(1) To buy national products, go to national product factories and national product companies with credibility and reputation.

(2) When buying national products, be sure to recognize the trademarks and styles that have a history and achievements to avoid being deceived and confused.

(3) Buying national products requires determination and a willingness to sacrifice, only then can it be effective.

(4) When buying national products, if you find a non-national product, do not condone or tolerate it so that unscrupulous merchants can succeed in their schemes.

(5) When buying national products, think that buying a national product is increasing the country's production power by one point. If you are not careful and buy an enemy product, it is like sending many bullets to them.

National Products Talk

Thinking of Some Remedial Measures From a Positive Perspective 162

— Ms. Jian Hua

The characteristic of women loving beauty is innate. And it is deeply rooted and unshakable. If you don't believe it, go to the streets or playgrounds and see. Not to mention women with some charm, everyone likes to put on powder, paint eyebrows, and dye nails. Even those Ugly women with pockmarked faces, protruding eyes, bald heads, and missing teeth, clearly become uglier with makeup, but they still desperately apply powder, curl their hair, spray perfume, and apply lipstick, thinking they are charming and moving. Almost every woman has this kind of self-pity and self-love. There is a sense of (I would rather have no ink in my chest than no powder on my face). Therefore, in recent months, no matter how much written persuasion or verbal explanation there is, saying that so much makeup is imported and advising them not to use foreign goods, they just (turn a deaf ear). Powder and perfume are still imported with increasing quantities. Therefore, I feel that negative obstruction is ineffective. We should still think of remedial measures from a positive perspective of encouraging the use of national products!

Chinese cosmetics have not been without progress in recent years. Except for the general aristocratic class who think it is not extravagant not to use them, most people use tooth powder and toothpaste such as Yonghe Industrial Company's Chang'e brand, Family Industry Society's Invincible brand, or China Chemical Industry Society's Samsung brand. As far as my family and several close relatives are concerned, we absolutely do not use foreign goods except for essential medicines. Cosmetics have been long-time customers of Invincible, Samsung, Guben, and other brands for more than ten years. Especially the products of Invincible brand, because the inventor is the literary scholar, scientist, and industrialist Tianxu Wosheng, we trust the things he supervises the most. Such as powder, snow cream, tooth powder, etc., there are definitely no drawbacks such as harming the skin or damaging teeth. And every time we go to his distribution office to visit, we always feel that there is progress every time. Various goods not only have improvements in substance from time to time, but also are becoming more and more beautiful in terms of decoration. We strive for beauty and can indeed compete with foreign goods. Other things such as Wuzhou Central and other factories' scented soaps and Samsung brand's toothpaste and snow cream are not inferior to imported goods. I very much hope that sisters will buy more, on the one hand, to promote national products, and on the other hand, to no longer bear the crime of being foreign goods salesmen. On the other hand, you can't see the amazing numbers of imported cosmetics. Three things can be achieved in one fell swoop. I think makeup sisters will definitely be happy to implement it! But here I have to declare that I am just a national product lover and have no advertising effect on the above-mentioned manufacturers. The reason why I want to list several brand names is because sisters only know that foreign goods are reliable with certain brands and numbers, and they don't know which national goods are better or worse. Therefore, I dare to introduce several more reliable ones based on my experience and ask sisters to buy them. Finally, if anyone publishes a list of the best manufacturers of daily necessities in this publication in the future (must not contain any advertising nature) so that national product lovers know where to go, this is also a way to promote national products.

In closing, I also hope that many of the best manufacturers of cosmetics will join hands with large companies such as Wing On, Sincere, Lai Wah, and Sun Sun. Each factory carefully selects a large number of goods and sends them to each company for display, and gives them preferential benefits to promote them widely. Most women like to shop at department stores. There are many foreign goods in the company, so they buy foreign goods together. If they are allowed to see a wide array of high-quality national products as soon as they enter the door, their vision and confidence can be attracted. Why don't the major manufacturers try it!

Wang Zirong (Middle) 163

— Ding Xing

(…Ladies and gentlemen, uncles, brothers and sisters, who would be willing to let your relatives be taken away, killed or humiliated? If this kind of situation really happened, who would not be willing to use force to rescue them? Now I am using the land within China's borders to compare to a person's relatives. The four northeastern provinces were easily taken away by the Japanese on September 18th without any effort, and we have no way to resist it. Some young patriots and the Northeastern Volunteer Army do not hesitate to sacrifice their flesh and blood to provide Japanese guns. I think this kind of meaningless sacrifice can also be said to be of little value. If there is sufficient preparation and there is indeed a possibility of defeating the enemy, then it may be worth attacking. Now, which aspect can be talked about? Having said that, are we just going to pass by silently? No! No! We should all stand up and do something that is even more powerful than using guns to fight them. On the one hand, those with capital should pool capital to establish national factories and expand factories to produce. On the other hand, all Chinese people should use national products. If we persist in this way for five or ten years, then there will be no foreign goods on the Chinese market. I think that although they are powerful, they will be fundamentally shaken because they have lost a good opportunity to sell goods in a dedicated market. Even if they come to invade, they will have no strength. Simply put, they use the surplus production of their countries to sell as much as possible to our country. Our people buy them, and a lot of money flows overseas, which is to provide them with a large amount of capital to build guns and cannons. If, as I said before, the Chinese people unanimously use Chinese goods, what are we afraid of them doing?…) At that time, tens of thousands of people were crowded together, concentrating and listening intently.

(Ladies and gentlemen! The four provinces of Liaoning and Jilin have gone. In the near future, I don't think they will be returned to us. Unless we work hard for the future, when they surrender later, they will naturally return things to their original owners. This all depends on the efforts of the public. This is what happened after the September 18th Incident in the 20th year of the Republic of China.

Educational News

Key Decisions of the International Professional and Technical Education Conference 164

The International Professional and Technical Education Conference is organized by France, Belgium, England, Germany, Italy, Spain, Egypt, Poland, and other countries. The president is the famous French scholar Mr. Nabes (Labbé). The inaugural meeting was held in Paris last year. The second international conference was held in Barcelona, Spain on May 17 this year. China was invited to participate by letter, but due to economic and time constraints, no representatives were sent. However, the Ministry of Education appointed Xie Shuying, section chief of the Higher Education Department, as a correspondent last year to communicate with the International Education Bureau at any time. (The bureau pays attention to international education news, and Mr. Xie is collecting materials to communicate with the bureau.) After the conference closed, the International Professional and Technical Education Bureau recently sent the main resolutions of the conference to the Ministry of Education. The original translation is very long. The following is an excerpt of its outline:

(1) The Trend of Vocational Education: The International Professional and Technical Education Conference (hereinafter referred to as "the Conference") believes that professional education and vocational education are very important from an economic and social standpoint and meet the needs of modern life. Therefore, all civilized countries have included this vocational education in their development plans. It is hoped that this type of education will obtain its due position in various countries.

(2) Vocational Guidance Methods: Because the education systems of some countries have not yet conformed to the International Labour Conference's proposed permissible age for children's work in stipulating children's schooling and permissible working age, it is hoped that professional education institutions will request the authorities to have appropriate regulations on children's working age and implement them immediately. On the one hand, during the years of compulsory education, in addition to teaching children the necessary general education, they should also be taught work skills so that children have the ability to choose skills and occupations.

Professional schools and the vocational world should strive to communicate and link up so that future vocational departments can be changed as needed by the times, and labour legislation should stipulate that all young workers must complete vocational education.

The International Professional and Technical Education Bureau should research the problems of vocational education that feel deficient in substance or spirit and investigate the methods of various countries that can solve this problem to remedy the deficiencies.

The Conference is deeply afraid that the results of vocational guidance will still not enable students leaving school to have a place to belong. Therefore, it is hoped that various places will borrow the strength of the government and organize several institutions within the scope permitted by national laws to accommodate those who have left primary school and are determined to learn skills, to provide them with employment guidance and to sincerely exercise the duties of guardians until the end of the learning period.

(3) Learning and Unemployment Issues: In terms of learning, technical learning, drawing, and factory practice should be closely linked. Internship work should be increased to quickly manufacture useful items. The Conference Committee hopes that at the next conference, it will take the opportunity to create a course work exhibition for mutual observation.

The Conference recognizes that unemployment poses a very serious danger to national culture. Therefore, it decided to adopt various effective methods such as (striving to adapt vocational education to the environment) and (creating special factories to cultivate vocational talents, etc.) to prevent various unemployment panics.

(4) Higher Professional Education Issues: The Conference believes that engineers with higher professional education can be cultivated through various methods, but they must all go through a sufficient period of study, receive considerable general education, and have the general professional knowledge that engineers must study. In addition, they must have expertise in their specialization. It is generally believed that the training of engineers should be carried out in schools with scientific training.

The Conference also recognizes that the number of technical talents is increasing day by day, their levels are uneven, and the difficulty of technicians seeking employment. Therefore, it decided that higher technical professional schools should adopt strict admission standards and that the issuance of graduation diplomas should be subject to strict government supervision. A part of those who study and learn on their own must have qualified academic ability and ability before they can apply for an engineer's certificate. At the same time, the outlets for engineers should be considered according to the needs of the industry to seek an appropriate supply and demand ratio.

The Conference conducted discussions on the management and protection of higher education and the position of engineers. It was generally believed that the profession of engineers is different from other liberal professions and has no national boundaries. It is proposed that the International Professional and Technical Education Bureau comprehensively compare the higher professional and technical education situation in various countries and formulate higher professional and technical education regulations and protection of academic degree regulations.

The Conference hopes that professional education will be divided into three levels in terms of the education system. The purpose of the first type of professional school is to create practical workers. The curriculum of the school has a broader scientific training than the former. The purpose is to create personnel with management and control capabilities. The third type of higher professional school enrolls students who have graduated from the previous two types of schools to receive deeper education and hopes to invite industrialists and industrial associations to participate in the board of directors of professional schools so that they can give instructions on the curriculum of professional schools.

(5) Contract Issues for Learning and Apprenticeships: The Conference believes that learning contracts should be a guarantee contract, an education contract, and the purpose is a standard for vocational training. It is hoped that this contract must be in writing to protect learners and apprentices from vocational training.

Zhou Fo Hai, Director of Education for Jiangsu Province, Addresses All Secondary School Students 165

(1) Hoping that diet, daily life, and actions conform to the principles of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame.

(2) Hoping to strive towards the two major goals of production and national defense.

Zhou Fo Hai, Director of Education for Jiangsu Province, addresses all secondary school students in Jiangsu in a letter, saying: Jiangsu's secondary education is known to be advanced. I, Fo Hai, upon appointment here, have the opportunity to meet and interact with students from all secondary schools in Jiangsu. I am sincerely pleased. From the beginning of my tenure, I deeply recognize the rampant study atmosphere and the declining moral principles as serious illnesses in today's school education. I intend to learn from the past and be cautious in the future to meet the expectations of the people of Jiangsu. Therefore, for those who incite disturbances and disrupt discipline, I will have to take decisive measures and impose strict sanctions with a heavy heart. After the pain subsides, I will repeatedly and earnestly persuade and emphasize the principle that studying is saving the country, and to save the country, one must study, showing students the correct path of learning. In recent years, the study atmosphere has changed for the better. The courage of the province's students to embrace good has truly given me boundless hopes. I cherish the youth and never advocate leniency. What I worry about day and night is how students can improve their studies, cultivate their character, strengthen their bodies, and whether they can recognize the mission of the times and shoulder the responsibility of saving the country. Leniency is no different from poison to the students; I will certainly not do that.

Using education to save the country is a consistent proposition for the whole country today, and it is also a truly effective and unchanging method. If one wants to achieve the effect of saving the country through education, the spiritual aspect must imbue education with the spirit of saving the country, and the material aspect must also prepare education for saving the country. In other words, education must become truly national-saving education and sweep away the emptiness of the past. I have long understood this. For several years, I have been striving with all my strength to promote and advance this kind of education. However, the target of education is all of our young students. If the students cannot thoroughly recognize their current responsibilities and work together to pursue the path of saving the country, then one-sided efforts will not help the reality. Therefore, in addition to my personal efforts, I must place this expectation on all students. At the beginning of the year, I am listing several points for the students to pay attention to.

Propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame are the basic conditions for being a person and the fundamental spirit for establishing a country. Without propriety and righteousness, there will be chaos between superiors and subordinates, and there will be no organization. Without integrity and shame, one will be perverse and do anything, and there will be no discipline. Once organization and discipline are lost, the country and nation will inevitably be in danger. The severity of China's national crisis today is due to this. Therefore, if we want to talk about saving the country through education today, we must use the entire educational force to revive our nation's inherent spirit of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame. There is no other way. Only with this spirit can we achieve education that saves the country; otherwise, it will be enough to destroy the country, let alone save it. What I hope for from the students today is not only the advancement of their studies but also the establishment of the basic conditions for being a person. If there is no cultivation of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame in school, then the conditions for being a person are incomplete. Even if one's studies are successful, it will not only be useless to the country and society but also contribute to wickedness and disorder. Knowing that being a person can be so harmful, the students should be aware and abide by school rules, pay attention to discipline, and obey the guidance of teachers. They should strive to improve themselves in everything, so that their diet, daily life, and all actions conform to the spirit of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, creating a new lifestyle. It must be known that intellectuals are the leaders of society. If all the intellectuals in the country can practice the life of propriety, righteousness, integrity, and shame, then the impact of their voices will create great power, and the foundation for the revival of the country and nation will not need to be sought elsewhere. I will devote my full efforts to continuous promotion and advancement. The students should also recognize the principles of being a person and automatically strive for the cultivation of their character, taking the lead in creating this atmosphere.

Saving the country cannot be achieved by empty talk; there must be sufficient preparation. Preparation of material strength is especially necessary. Therefore, today's education should focus on the two central goals of production and national defense. Education that does not have the effect of production will inevitably be empty. Education that does not contribute to national defense is tantamount to being useless. Empty and useless education is certainly not enough to save the country. I have spared no effort to adopt any effective methods to change the direction of education. The facts are there, and I believe you are well aware. What I hope for from the students is to work hard towards these two major goals, so that education can achieve the practical effect of saving the country. In terms of production, there are both positive and negative meanings. The positive aspect is the cultivation of production skills and the development of a work ethic. The negative aspect is suppressing material desires and reducing personal consumption. This is the true spirit of today's school education, and it is what the students should deeply recognize and automatically strive to realize. In terms of national defense, the students cannot immediately make significant contributions. However, national defense depends on science. Changes in the situation of the borderlands and the assessment of the enemy's and our own national conditions depend on the study of history and geography. The invention of defensive and offensive weapons, as well as the application of new tactics, are closely related to training in subjects such as physics, chemistry, and military affairs. By analogy, almost every subject is related to national defense. If the students lay a solid foundation for science today, it will be no different from the entire nation broadly reserving basic tools for national defense. I deeply hope that they will continuously research with a spirit of initiative, gradually progressing from experimental steps to creation. Paying attention to physical education and striving for military training is sufficient to strengthen physical fitness and break the habit of being weak. In the event of war, it is even sufficient to defend the country and protect the nation. Its contribution to national defense is even more practical. All of these are what the students should strive for in school today, and it is by no means a harsh requirement from me.

In short, the crisis of the country and nation today is imminent. The only thing we can rely on to save the country and maintain the survival of the nation is education. If we want to achieve the practical effect of saving the country through education, we must change our course and imbue education with the spirit of saving the country and the preparation of material strength. If I cannot recognize the importance of national-saving education and do my best to promote it internally, then it is my fault. If the students cannot thoroughly recognize their current responsibilities and work together to pursue the path of saving the country, then the students will be abandoning their duty, and there will be no escaping blame. It is my duty to supervise and urge each other and never be lenient, so as not to mislead the students and mislead the entire country and nation. The words are earnest and sincere; put them into practice and do not slacken. September 1, 1934.

Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education Bans Substandard Private Primary Schools 168

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education, upon investigation of the Jianwen Private Primary School in Chunhui Lane, Aierjin Road, and the Cihua Private Primary School in Qingshan Lane, Aierjin Road, found that the facilities were simple, the order was chaotic, and the teaching was ineffective. Furthermore, the board of directors and the schools had not applied for registration. According to Article 30, Paragraph 1 of the revised regulations for private schools, the two schools have been strictly ordered by the bureau to cease operations and report within one month.

Measures for Religious Organizations to Run Educational Undertakings 169

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education Announces an Interpretation Based on an Order from the Ministry of Education

The Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education recently received an interpretation from the Ministry of Education regarding the meaning of the phrase "one organization" in Item 2 of the Measures for Religious Organizations to Run Educational Undertakings and notified all schools as follows: According to the instruction No. 10702 from the Ministry of Education, "The Measures for Religious Organizations to Run Educational Undertakings were previously formulated by the Ministry and promulgated in April of the 18th year, with orders for compliance. Subsequently, the Education Department of Zhejiang Province requested an interpretation of the meaning of the phrase 'organization' in Item 2 of the measures. The interpretation given was that the phrase 'organization' refers to churches, temples, or societies and training centers established by believers of various religions for the purpose of preaching and explaining doctrines, focusing on religious teachings, etc., etc., etc., etc., etc. Recently, it has been found that some religious organizations are still establishing organizations under their own names. Although they do not use the name of schools on the surface, they are actually school organizations, which is inappropriate. It is now clearly stipulated that religious organizations establishing schools should follow the revised regulations for private schools. If they establish organizations to transmit religious doctrines, they must not use the name of schools, nor imitate school regulations, compile curricula, enroll school-age children, or youths under the age of eighteen, and teach subjects that should be taught in primary and secondary schools, in order to prevent misuse and avoid confusion. In addition to this announcement, it is hereby ordered that compliance be followed and further ordered for compliance."

China Educational Film Association Sub-Leases Educational Films from the League of Nations 170

All Educational Institutions Can Rent from the Association

The China Educational Film Association recently rented thirty sets of educational films from the International Educational Film Association of the League of Nations. All domestic educational institutions and schools can rent from the association. The rental methods and film names are listed below:

Rental Methods: (1) Educational institutions or schools renting educational films from the League of Nations must contact the Nanjing headquarters of the China Educational Film Association. (2) Educational institutions or schools renting the aforementioned films must be responsible for care and safekeeping. (3) The aforementioned thirty sets of films are divided into six groups, each group charging a rental fee of fifteen yuan per day of screening. Renting all of them costs ninety yuan, to be paid in one lump sum. (4) The aforementioned thirty sets of films are screened in rotation within each institution or school in six groups. The order is arranged by the Nanjing headquarters of the China Educational Film Association. (5) The postage for sending the films back and forth is borne by the institution or school renting the films. If two or more institutions or schools in the same area rent the aforementioned films at the same time, the postage is borne jointly by the two or more institutions or schools in that area. (6) The institution or school renting the films should take good care of the films. If there is any damage, compensation must be paid at the price.

Film Names: Historical Rome, Eye Surgery, Tree Oil Makes Brass Wire, Gurigi Lamp, Jumping Common Patients with Lung Disease, Flowing Gas Steel, Religious Festival, Egg to Chicken, Bee Life, Wood Nan Luo Glass Manufacturing, Flies, Plant Life, Living Crystals, Seaside Garden, Planet Ten Thousand, Crystalline Phenomena, 19th Century Dejing, Canaera Marble Production, Milky Way Wonders, Soap Bubbles, Sriwin Peak, Great St. Banner Robbery, Wheat, Wash Hands Before Grafting, Respirator, Large and Small Others,

The High School Department of Fudan University is Renamed Fudan Senior High School 172

The high school department of Fudan University was formerly the preparatory course of Fudan University. In the 21st year, it was renamed Jiangwan High School Department. All administrative matters were coordinated with the Xujiahui Affiliated Middle School. However, because the Ministry of Education promulgated revised regulations for various schools, middle schools are not allowed to establish branch schools, but should be established separately and independently. The school affairs meeting decided to rename it Fudan Senior High School. Subsequently, the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Education was requested to change the name, and it is said that approval has been granted.

China Public School Opens 173

China Public School has started classes on the 24th of this month. This semester, the curriculum has been slightly reorganized. The news is recorded as follows:

New Professors Hired: This semester, the school has new courses and has hired new professors, most of whom are well-known figures. In the Department of Literature, Le Sibing teaches Phonology, Chuan Yanchang teaches Nationalism, History of the Orient, and Literary Criticism, Wu Jingshan teaches Local History Research, and Xiong Zirong teaches Vocational Education. In the Department of Political Economy, Ben Quanshi teaches Public Finance, Wang Fuyan teaches Comparative Constitution, Cheng Dexu teaches Comparative Government, and Zhu Tongyi teaches Labor Economics and History of Economic Thought. In the Department of Commerce, Wang Zhongchang teaches Statistics, etc.

Military Training: This semester, the school is following the orders of the Ministry of Education and has appointed Mr. He Shufan to be in charge of military training. Currently, all students in the school are uniformly preparing uniforms and are divided into classes for training. Both academic and technical subjects are strictly required to cultivate the spirit of military citizenship.

The Public Concession Labor Bureau has been running a normal school for many years, its purpose being to train Chinese people to be able to serve as English teachers. In addition to enrolling students from the Labor Bureau's various schools for training, the school also enrolls qualified students from outside. This season, the normal class is scheduled to start on October 8th. For students attending, the tuition fee is ten yuan per semester for one subject and fifteen yuan for more than one subject. Class time is Monday, Tuesday, Wednesday, and Friday from 5:00 PM to 7:00 PM. The school address is attached to the Yucai Public School on Shanhai Guan Road. Those who wish to register or inquire about details should go to the school between 5:00 PM and 7:00 PM on Friday, October 5th, to contact the teacher in charge of the normal class.

Letter from Huang Jingwan 179

I have read the news item "Second Anniversary of the Shanhai Industrial School Group" published in your newspaper on the 26th of this month, which states that it was founded by me. This is clearly inconsistent with the facts. Upon investigation, the founder of the group was the rural educator Dr. Tao Zhixing, who painstakingly managed it with more than 3,000 yuan from his manuscript fees to experiment with life education. There is no work-study program. Although I know it well, I have not made any donations and dare not take credit for it. I hereby make this correction. Huang Jingwan.

Datong University Implements Universal Physical Education 188

Fang Wanbang Hired to Preside

A New Atmosphere Implemented for Three Weeks

Since last year, Datong University has implemented various plans as part of its national rejuvenation education initiative, paying particular attention to student physical education. Beginning this autumn, to correct the flaws in athletes' sports, the university hired physical education expert Fang Wanbang as Director of Physical Education, who detailed a plan for universal physical education. After only three weeks of implementation, the entire school has a new atmosphere. The main facilities are listed below:

Five Objectives (1) To provide all students with suitable sports opportunities to ensure healthy physical and mental development; (2) To teach movement skills necessary for daily life, recreation, art, national defense; (3) To cultivate a love and appreciation for physical activity; (4) To cultivate cooperation, unity, fairness, courage, chivalry, diligence, and endurance, to complete moral and character education; (5) To improve poor physical development.

Course Types The school varies its content according to the students' gender, ability, interest, and physique. For morning exercises, boys focus on German gymnastics, imitation exercises, and natural activities, while girls focus on Danish gymnastics, German gymnastics, and natural activities. Extracurricular activities for boys include football, basketball, volleyball, tennis, baseball, handball, cage ball, track and field, martial arts, swimming, group games, field activities, and light and heavy apparatus exercises. Extracurricular activities for girls include volleyball, basketball, tennis, softball, dance, archery, martial arts, track and field, swimming, group games, and field activities.

Facilities Overview The school campus covers more than 300 acres and boasts spacious sports fields. Currently, there is one football field (shared with morning exercises and baseball), six basketball courts, six tennis courts, eight volleyball courts, one track and field, one 400-meter running track, one handball field, six heavy apparatus, two martial arts fields, and one group game field for boys. For girls, there is one morning exercise field (shared with softball), three basketball courts, two volleyball courts, one tennis court, one archery field, and one group game field. All sports equipment for ball games and track and field is very complete.

Competition Methods Morning exercises are temporarily designated as a required course for first and second-year students, divided into boys' and girls' sections. Every morning at 7:00 AM, students line up in order, and each assistant teacher takes attendance before starting the exercise for 20 minutes. Extracurricular activities are a required course for all students, held every afternoon. The first session runs from 4:00 PM to 4:40 PM, and the second session runs from 5:00 PM to 5:40 PM. Each student selects their group time and activity type during registration and is then assigned by the Physical Education Department. Assessment of performance is based on diligence, sportsmanship, attitude, and skill progress. Award methods are divided into group and individual. Group awards include inter-college competitions, grade-level competitions, team competitions, and field trips. Individual awards include various medals, tests, and skills competitions. The school will hold two school-wide sports meets in the spring and autumn of each year, as well as friendly competitions with other schools. It is reported that all championships will not be participated in.

French Barracks Athletic Association Launches Amateur Jai Alai Tournament 189

Open to All Nationalities

Since the introduction of Jai Alai from Europe through the Central Sports Ground in this city several years ago, Shanghai residents have become very interested in it. Therefore, the number of people practicing this sport is increasing day by day. However, due to a lack of promotion, the organization of amateur Jai Alai clubs in Shanghai and the launch of open amateur championships have not yet been carried out. Now, the French Barracks Athletic Association, in view of this, has specially launched a campaign to collect prizes from all walks of life and host the Shanghai Open Amateur Jai Alai Single, Double, and Triple Championships. Regardless of nationality, all can participate. According to this move, it is still an innovative concept in the sports world. Those who have this hobby are encouraged to participate actively and work together to make it a success. The participation requirements for this competition are as follows: (1) Any non-professional Jai Alai player, regardless of nationality, may participate. (2) There are three types: Single, Double, and Triple. Those participating in Doubles and Triples must participate in the name of a group, and those participating in Singles may participate in their own name. (3) The participation fee for Triples is five yuan per group, three yuan for Doubles, and one yuan for Singles. If you participate in all the competitions in the name of a group, the total fee is five yuan, to show preferential treatment. (A group of three can participate, those participating in all the competitions can participate in one group of Triples, one group of Doubles, and three groups of Singles.) (4) From now until 11:00 AM on September 30, please contact Mr. Wang Jiesheng of the Nanjing Road China Photo Studio with your registration photo (regardless of 2 inches or 4 inches) every day from 9:30 AM to 11:00 AM in the morning and 2:30 PM to 4:00 PM in the afternoon. (5) The court is the French Barracks Indoor Jai Alai Court at No. 199 Jinshenfu Road. Hard balls are used, weighing 95 centimeters. The ball basket must be provided by yourself. Please inquire about the court rules when registering.

In various cities and villages in Fuyang, this year's autumn silkworms have been affected by the weather, with drought causing disasters, mulberry leaves withering and yellowing. Later, the weather was abnormal, with continuous rain and sultry heat, and both early and late silkworms were damaged. The early fresh cocoons have already been on the market, and the cocoon price is only 20 yuan at most and 14 yuan at least due to the control. The current situation of the late silkworms is better, and they can go to the cluster soon. It is estimated that the cocoon production will be at most 60% of the usual amount.
